  "document_summary": "This document is issue 1724 of the official gazette \"Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm,\" published on February 2, 2025. It compiles a wide range of official government decrees, decisions, and announcements from various ministries and public authorities in Kuwait. Key content includes ministerial decrees on higher education and information, decisions from the Capital Markets Authority regarding financial licenses, and numerous decrees from the Central Bank of Kuwait concerning financial institutions and exchange companies. A significant portion is dedicated to tender announcements and postponements from entities like the Amiri Diwan, Central Agency for Public Tenders, and Ministries of Interior, Defense, Health, and Finance, covering diverse projects from infrastructure to medical supplies. Additionally, the gazette features legal announcements such as criminal judgments, property auctions, company liquidations and registrations, commercial agency updates, and reports from committees on births, deaths, and name corrections, reflecting a comprehensive overview of governmental and commercial activities in Kuwait.",

# Ministry of Higher Education / Wizarat Al-Ta'leem Al-Ali <orig>وزارة التعليم العالي</orig>
## Ministerial Resolution No. (39/2025)
Regarding the addition of certain study programs and academic degrees to the list of higher education institutions approved for enrollment in Bachelor's and postgraduate programs in the Kingdom of Saudi Arabia.
- Having reviewed Decree-Law No. 15 of 1979 concerning Civil Service and its amending laws.

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
</header>

- And on the Decree issued on April 4, 1979, regarding the Civil Service System and its amendments.
- And on Amiri Decree No. (417) of 2010, issued on October 25, 2010, regarding the establishment of the National Bureau for Academic Accreditation and Education Quality Assurance / Al-Jihaz Al-Watani lil-I'timad Al-Akadimi wa Dhaman Jawdat Al-Ta'lim <orig>الجهاز الوطني للاعتماد الأكاديمي وضمان جودة التعليم</orig>.
- And on Ministerial Resolution No. (272) issued on October 3, 2012, regarding allowing Kuwaiti students to enroll for study outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> only in universities for which a ministerial resolution is issued by the National Bureau for Academic Accreditation and Education Quality Assurance / Al-Jihaz Al-Watani lil-I'timad Al-Akadimi wa Dhaman Jawdat Al-Ta'lim <orig>الجهاز الوطني للاعتماد الأكاديمي وضمان جودة التعليم</orig>.
- And on Academic Resolution No. (2014/7) issued on May 14, 2014, regarding allowing students wishing to study Bachelor's and postgraduate programs in the Kingdom of Saudi Arabia <orig>المملكة العربية السعودية</orig> to enroll in the higher education institutions listed in the resolution.
- And on the resolution of the Board of Directors of the National Bureau for Academic Accreditation and Education Quality Assurance / Al-Jihaz Al-Watani lil-I'timad Al-Akadimi wa Dhaman Jawdat Al-Ta'lim <orig>الجهاز الوطني للاعتماد الأكاديمي وضمان جودة التعليم</orig> No. (7) issued on December 31, 2014, which includes the mechanism for issuing resolutions related to identifying higher education institutions outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> whose graduates' qualifications are permitted to be accredited.
- And on the resolution of the Board of Directors of the National Bureau for Academic Accreditation and Education Quality Assurance / Al-Jihaz Al-Watani lil-I'timad Al-Akadimi wa Dhaman Jawdat Al-Ta'lim <orig>الجهاز الوطني للاعتماد الأكاديمي وضمان جودة التعليم</orig> No. (2014/5) regarding the criteria for selecting higher education institutions outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>.
- And on Academic Resolution No. (2015/199) issued on June 11, 2015, regarding the addition of Alfaisal University <orig>جامعة الفيصل</orig> to the list of permitted higher education institutions for enrollment, as listed in Academic Resolution No. (2014/7) dated May 14, 2014, for studying Bachelor's programs only, excluding medical specializations.
- And on Ministerial Resolution No. (2022/55) issued on March 21, 2022, regarding the registration and enrollment of Kuwaiti students in the Bachelor of Medicine and Surgery program at Alfaisal University <orig>جامعة الفيصل</orig> in the Kingdom of Saudi Arabia <orig>المملكة العربية السعودية</orig>.

# Ministry of Information / Wizarat Al-I'lam <orig>وزارة الإعلام</orig>
## Administrative Decision No. (6) of 2025
Regarding the cancellation of the license for the electronic media outlet named (Al-Waseet Newspaper / Jaridat Al-Waseet <orig>جريدة الوسيط</orig>)
Assistant Undersecretary for Press, Publishing and Printed Materials Sector Affairs:
Having reviewed:
- Law No. (8) of 2016 regulating electronic media.
- Ministerial Resolution No. (100) of 2016 issuing the executive regulations for Law No. 8 of 2016 regulating electronic media.
- Administrative Decision No. (80) of 2023 regarding the cancellation of Al-Waseet Newspaper's <orig>جريدة الوسيط</orig> license.
- Administrative Decision No. 655 of 2022 regarding the delegation of certain competencies.
- Electronic Media License No. 2019/368 issued on 22/12/2019.
- Letter from the Director of the Electronic Publishing Department No. 13 dated 21/1/2025.
- And what the public interest dictates.
Has decided:
**Article One**
License No. 2019/368 for the electronic media outlet "Al-Waseet Newspaper / Jaridat Al-Waseet <orig>جريدة الوسيط</orig>" is hereby cancelled by operation of law, in implementation of Article (16), Clause 2 of Law No. 8 of 2016 regulating electronic media.
**Article Two**
Those concerned shall be notified of this decision, and it shall be published on the Ministry's official website and in the Official Gazette.
Assistant Undersecretary
for Press, Publishing and Printed Materials Sector

Issued on: 27 Rajab 1446 AH

  "page_title": "Ministerial Decrees: Master's Program in Speech and Language Pathology and Amendment to Traffic Council Resolution <orig>قرارات وزارية: برنامج ماجستير في أمراض النطق واللغة وتعديل قرار المجلس الأعلى للمرور</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-02-02",

  "publisher": "Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page of Al-Kuwait Al-Youm official gazette features two ministerial decrees: one from the Ministry of Higher Education regarding the addition of a Master's program in Speech and Language Pathology, and another from the Ministry of Interior amending Ministerial Resolution No. 2022/254 concerning the Supreme Traffic Council."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
3
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue No. 1724, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
</header>

*   Based on the recommendation of the Committee for Setting Standards and Identifying Higher Education Institutions in Medical Specialties and Programs Outside the State of Kuwait <orig>لجنة وضع معايير وتحديد مؤسسات التعليم العالي في التخصصات والبرامج الطبية خارج دولة الكويت</orig> at its fifty-fourth meeting held on December 18, 2024.
*   Based on the presentation of the Director General of the National Bureau for Academic Accreditation and Education Quality Assurance <orig>الجهاز الوطني للاعتماد الأكاديمي وضمان جودة التعليم</orig>.
*   And as required by the public interest.

Decided

## Article One
To add the Master's program in Clinical Speech and Language Pathology <orig>علم أمراض النطق واللغة السريرية</orig> at Alfaisal University <orig>جامعة الفيصل</orig> to Academic Resolution No. (2014/7) issued on May 14, 2014, which permits enrollment for Bachelor's and postgraduate programs in the Kingdom of Saudi Arabia.

## Article Two
Study must be conducted through regular attendance during the academic week, and the study program in which students enroll must follow the traditional education system.

## Article Three
The study program in which students enroll must have completed the specified study period for granting the academic degree, by graduating the first cohort from the college offering this program.

## Article Four
Resolutions regulating enrollment and the study system in educational institutions outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> must be observed. It must also be observed that academic degrees have met the requirements for their acquisition in accordance with the regulating resolutions issued by the Ministry of Higher Education <orig>وزارة التعليم العالي</orig> in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>.

## Article Five
This Resolution shall be effective from its date of issuance, and any text contradicting its provisions shall be revoked. It shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

## Article Six
The competent authorities shall be informed and act accordingly.

Minister of Higher Education and Scientific Research <orig>وزير التعليم العالي والبحث العلمي</orig>
Dr. Nader Abdullah Mohammed Al-Jalal <orig>د. نادر عبد الله محمد الجلال</orig>

<footer>
Issued on: 23 Rajab 1446 AH
Corresponding to: January 23, 2025 AD
</footer>

---

# Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
## (Ministerial Resolution No. 76 of 2025)
### Regarding: Amendment of a Resolution

First Deputy Prime Minister and Minister of Defense and Minister of Interior <orig>النائب الأول لرئيس مجلس الوزراء ووزير الدفاع ووزير الداخلية</orig>

*   Having reviewed Decree-Law No. 67/76 <orig>المرسوم بقانون رقم 67/76</orig> concerning Traffic and its amendments.
*   And Ministerial Resolution No. 81/76 <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم 81/76</orig> concerning the Executive Regulations of the Traffic Law and its amendments.
*   And Ministerial Resolution No. 2022/254 <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم 2022/254</orig> concerning the Supreme Traffic Council <orig>المجلس الأعلى للمرور</orig> and its amendment.
*   And the letter from the Assistant Undersecretary for Traffic and Operations Affairs <orig>وكيل الوزارة المساعد لشئون المرور والعمليات</orig> No. 6 dated 8/1/2025 AD.
*   And based on the presentation of the Undersecretary <orig>وكيل الوزارة</orig>.

Has decided

## Article (1)
Item No. (11) of Article No. (1) of the aforementioned Ministerial Resolution No. 2022/254 <orig>القرار الوزاري رقم 2022/254</orig> shall be amended to read as follows: -
- 11- Brigadier General (Legal) / Khalid Abdullah Misfer Al-Adwani <orig>العميد حقوقي/ خالد عبدالله مسفر العدواني</orig> – Secretary

## Article (2)
The Undersecretary <orig>وكيل الوزارة</orig> shall implement this Resolution, which shall be effective from its date of issuance and published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

First Deputy Prime Minister <orig>النائب الأول لرئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig>
And Minister of Defense and Minister of Interior <orig>ووزير الدفاع ووزير الداخلية</orig>
Fahad Yusuf Saud Al-Sabah <orig>فهد يوسف سعود الصباح</orig>

It was decided as follows:
### Article One:

## Decision No. (16) of 2025
Regarding
A Private Marketing License for a Collective Investment Scheme Established Outside the State of Kuwait Granted to Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig> for Marketing Shares of MKZ Development 45 Company <orig>شركة إم كي زي ديفيلوبمنت 45</orig>

- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, its Executive Regulations, and their amendments;
- The Articles of Association and Memorandum of Incorporation of Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig>, and the agreement concluded between the representative of the collective investment scheme, Markaz Investment Advisors Ltd, and the marketing manager, Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig>;

- And based on Decision No. (04) of 2025 regarding the amendment of final approval powers for the work procedures of the Supervision Sector, issued on 12/01/2025.

It was decided as follows:
### Article One:
Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig> is licensed to privately market 35,000 shares (thirty-five thousand shares only) of MKZ Development 45 Company <orig>شركة إم كي زي ديفيلوبمنت 45</orig> within the State of Kuwait, which originated in the Cayman Islands, and the offer price shall be EUR 1,000 (one thousand Euros only) per share.

### Article Two:
The shares to be marketed within the State of Kuwait shall be offered only to professional clients as per the text in Book One (Definitions) of the Executive Regulations of Law No. 7 of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, and their amendments, and the entity

# Decision No. (18) of 2025
## Regarding
**Renewal of Securities Activities License for KFH Capital Brokerage Company <orig>شركة كفيك للوساطة المالية</orig>**

**Having reviewed:**
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, its Executive Regulations, and their amendments;
- The Securities Activities License Certificate for KFH Capital Brokerage Company <orig>شركة كفيك للوساطة المالية</orig> No. (0005/AP/2013) issued on 13/04/2022;
- The request from KFH Capital Brokerage Company <orig>شركة كفيك للوساطة المالية</orig> for the renewal of its securities activities license with the Authority;
- And based on Decision No. (4) of 2025 regarding the amendment of final approval powers for the operational procedures of the Supervision Sector <orig>قطاع الإشراف</orig>, issued on 12/01/2025.

**Decided the following:**
### Article One
The securities activities license for KFH Capital Brokerage Company <orig>شركة كفيك للوساطة المالية</orig> with the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> is renewed for carrying out the activity of a registered securities broker on the Securities Exchange <orig>بورصة الأوراق المالية</orig>.
This is for a period of three years, renewable, effective from 11/04/2025.

### Article Two
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall be effective from its date of issuance and published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

# Resolution No. (20) of 2025
## Regarding
Private Marketing License for a Collective Investment Scheme Established Outside the State of Kuwait Granted to Bayt Al-Awraq Al-Maliya Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig> for Marketing Units of USIBA 4 Real Estate Fund

## Having reviewed:
*   Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, its Executive Regulations, and amendments thereof;
*   The Articles of Association and Memorandum of Incorporation of Bayt Al-Awraq Al-Maliya Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig>, and the agreement concluded between the collective investment scheme Blue Pillar Advisors Ltd and the marketing manager Bayt Al-Awraq Al-Maliya Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig>;
*   The request from Bayt Al-Awraq Al-Maliya Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig> to undertake the private marketing of units of the USIBA 4 Real Estate Fund;
*   And based on Resolution No. (04) of 2025 regarding the amendment of final approval authorities for the work procedures of the Supervision Sector, issued on 12/01/2025.

## Has resolved the following:

### Article One
Bayt Al-Awraq Al-Maliya Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig> is licensed to privately market 25,000 units (only twenty-five thousand units) of the USIBA 4 Real Estate Fund within the State of Kuwait, established in the Cayman Islands. Each unit consists of the following:
1.  1 share (one share) whose holder does not have voting rights in USIBA 4 Real Estate Ltd.
2.  3 shares (three shares) whose holders do not have voting rights in USIBA 4 Finance Ltd.
The offer price shall be 4,000 US Dollars (only four thousand US Dollars) per unit, in addition to a subscription commission of 1% payable once upon subscription.

### Article Three
The objectives of the collective investment scheme shall be determined based on what is stated in the prospectus.

### Article Four
The marketing license duration is one year, renewable annually, starting from the date of issuance of the Authority's license certificate and after payment of the prescribed fees.

### Article Five
The prescribed fees shall be paid within one month from the date of issuance of this Resolution. In case of failure to pay the fees within the specified period, the Resolution shall be deemed null and void.

### Article Six
The competent authorities shall implement this Resolution, each within its jurisdiction. It shall be effective from its date of issuance and published in the Official Gazette.

<footer>
Acting Head of the Supervision Sector
Fahad Abdullah Al-Fadhli <orig>فهد عبد الله الفضلي</orig>
Issued on: January 28, 2025 AD
</footer>

# Resolution No. (21) of 2025
## Regarding
A Private Marketing License for a Collective Investment Scheme Established
Outside the State of Kuwait Granted to National Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig>
For Marketing Shares of the Tenth Islamic Ijarah and Finance Fund Company <orig>شركة صندوق الإجارة والتمويل الإسلامي العاشر بالدينار الكويتي المحدود</orig>
(Kuwaiti Dinar Limited)

Having reviewed:
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, its Executive Regulations, and their amendments;
- The Articles of Association and Bylaws of National Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig>, and the agreement concluded between the representative of the collective investment scheme, Intervest LP <orig>إنتر فست إل بي</orig>, and the marketing manager, National Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig>;
- The request from National Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig> to undertake the private marketing of shares of the Tenth Islamic Ijarah and Finance Fund Company <orig>شركة صندوق الإجارة والتمويل الإسلامي العاشر بالدينار الكويتي المحدود</orig> (Kuwaiti Dinar Limited);
- Based on Resolution No. (04) of 2025 regarding the amendment of final approval authorities for the operational procedures of the Supervision Sector <orig>قطاع الإشراف</orig>, issued on 2025/01/12.

It has been resolved as follows:

### Article One
National Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig> is licensed to privately market 500,000 shares (five hundred thousand shares only) of the shares of the Tenth Islamic Ijarah and Finance Fund Company <orig>شركة صندوق الإجارة والتمويل الإسلامي العاشر بالدينار الكويتي المحدود</orig> (Kuwaiti Dinar Limited) within the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, which is established in the Cayman Islands. The offer price shall be 100 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (one hundred Kuwaiti Dinars only) per share, in addition to a subscription commission of up to 2.25% payable once upon subscription.

### Article Two
The shares to be marketed within the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> shall be offered exclusively to professional clients, as stipulated in Book One (Definitions) of the Executive Regulations of Law No. 7 of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, and their amendments. The entity receiving subscription requests shall be:
- Securities House Company <orig>شركة بيت الأوراق المالية</orig>.

### Article Three
The objectives of the collective investment scheme shall be determined based on what is stated in the prospectus.

### Article Four
The marketing license duration is one year, renewable annually, commencing from the date of issuance of the Authority's <orig>الهيئة</orig> license certificate and after payment of the prescribed fees.

### Article Five
The prescribed fees shall be paid within one month from the date of issuance of this resolution. In case of failure to pay the fees within the specified period, the resolution shall be deemed null and void.

### Article Six
The competent authorities shall implement this resolution, each within its jurisdiction. It shall be effective from its date of issuance and published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

Acting Head of the Supervision Sector <orig>قطاع الإشراف</orig>
Fahad Abdullah Al-Fadhli <orig>فهد عبد الله الفضلي</orig>
<footer>
Issued on: January 28, 2025 AD
</footer>Capital Markets <orig>أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, and their amendments. The entities receiving subscription requests shall be:
- National Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig>.

# Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>
## Decision No. 1 / 4 - R / 2025

Governor of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>
Having reviewed Articles (21) and (61) of Law No. (32) of 1968 regarding Currency, the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>, and the Regulation of the Banking Profession and its amendments.
And Articles (4), (5), (7) of Ministerial Decision No. (39) of 2003 regarding the regulation of the banks' register system at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.
And based on the request of the Industrial Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الصناعي</orig> dated 29/12/2024 regarding the amendment of its data in the banks' register at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.

Has decided:

### Article One
The following amendments to the data of the Industrial Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الصناعي</orig> shall be recorded in the banks' register at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>:
1- The termination of membership of the following non-independent Board of Directors members:
- Musab Salem Al-Nisf <orig>مصعب سالم النصف</orig>.
- Al-Jazi Ali Al-Mashout <orig>الجازي علي المشوط</orig>.
- Basma Ahmed Al-Farsi <orig>بسمة أحمد الفارسي</orig>.
- Rasha Fahad Al-Amir <orig>رشا فهد الأمير</orig>.
2- The appointment of the following non-independent Board of Directors members to complete the current term (2023-2025):
- Hadeel Faisal Boukhadour <orig>هديل فيصل بوخضور</orig>.
- Dalal Hamed Mandani <orig>دلال حامد مندني</orig>.
- Abdullah Ibrahim Al-Khashti <orig>عبدالله إبراهيم الخشتي</orig>.
- Lulwa Abdul Latif Al-Dharban <orig>لولوة عبداللطيف الذربان</orig>.
3- The re-formation of the Board of Directors members of the Industrial Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الصناعي</orig> for the current term (2023-2025) from the following individuals:

## Decision No. 1 / 7 - R / 2025
### Governor of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>
Having reviewed Article (21) of Law No. (32) of 1968 regarding Currency, the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>, and the Regulation of the Banking Profession, and its amendments.
And Articles (7), (10) of the Ministerial Decision of 1984 regarding subjecting exchange companies to the supervision of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.
And based on the request of Bahrain Exchange Company <orig>شركة البحرين للصرافة</orig> dated 1/12/2025 regarding the amendment of its data in the register of exchange companies at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.
Has decided
### Article One
The following amendments to the data of Bahrain Exchange Company <orig>شركة البحرين للصرافة</orig> shall be recorded in the register of exchange companies at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>:
- Opening of a new branch for the company in Al-Shaddadiya Industrial Area <orig>منطقة الشدادية الصناعية</orig> – Plot (1) – Parcel (900001) – Al-Shaddadiya Expatriate Labor Accommodation Building <orig>مبنى سكن العمالة الوافدة الشدادية</orig> – Unit No. (7) – Automated Address Number (22051554).
- Opening of a new branch for the company in Al-Shaddadiya Industrial Area <orig>منطقة الشدادية الصناعية</orig> – Plot (1) – Parcel (900001) – Al-Shaddadiya Expatriate Labor Accommodation Building <orig>مبنى سكن العمالة الوافدة الشدادية</orig> – Unit No. (7) – Automated Address Number (22051749).
### Article Two
This Decision shall be published in the Official Gazette and shall come into effect from the date of its issuance.

## Decision No. 1 / 8 - R / 2025
### Governor of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>
Having reviewed Articles (21) and (61) of Law No. (32) of 1968 regarding Currency, the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>, and the Regulation of the Banking Profession, and its amendments.
And Articles (4), (5), and (7) of Ministerial Decision No. (39) of 2003 regarding the Regulations for the Register of Banks at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.
And based on the request of National Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الوطني</orig> dated 1/8/2025 regarding the amendment of its data in the register of banks at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.
Has decided
### Article One
The following amendment to the data of National Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الوطني</orig> shall be recorded in the register of banks at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>:
- Closure of the bank branch located in Al-Shuwaikh Area <orig>منطقة الشويخ</orig> – Mobile Telecommunications Company Building <orig>مبنى شركة الاتصالات المتنقلة</orig> – Ground Floor.
### Article Two
This Decision shall be published in the Official Gazette and shall come into effect from the date of its issuance.
<footer>
The Governor

Corresponding to: 22 January 2025 AD

# Resolution No. 1 / 10 / R / 2025
## Governor of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>
Having reviewed Article (21) of Law No. (32) of 1968 regarding currency, the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>, the regulation of the banking profession, and its amendments.
And Articles (7) and (10) of the Ministerial Resolution of 1984 regarding subjecting exchange companies to the supervision of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.
And based on the request of Aman Exchange Company <orig>شركة أمان للصرافة</orig> dated 2025/1/14 concerning the amendment of its data in the register of exchange companies at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>.
It was resolved
### Article One
The following amendment shall be recorded in the register of exchange companies at the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig> regarding the data of Aman Exchange Company <orig>شركة أمان للصرافة</orig>:

### Article Two
This resolution shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> and shall be effective from the date of its issuance.
The Governor

# Resolution No. 1 / 9 / R / 2025
## Governor of the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>
Having reviewed Articles (21) and (61) of Law No. (32) of 1968 regarding currency, the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig>, the regulation of the banking profession, and its amendments.

### Article One

The Governor

**Error:**
- And on electronic media license No. 2016/40 issued on 29/11/2021.

**Correct:**
- And on electronic media license No. 2016/40 issued on 29/11/2016.

Therefore, we are re-publishing the administrative decision after correcting the aforementioned error.

# Administrative Decision No. (4) of 2025
## Regarding the Cancellation of the Electronic Media Outlet License
## Under the Name (Al-Kuwaitiya Newspaper <orig>جريدة الكويتية</orig>)
Assistant Undersecretary for Press, Publishing and Printed Materials Sector Affairs:

**Having reviewed:**
- Law No. (8) of 2016 regarding the regulation of electronic media,
- Ministerial Decision No. (100) of 2016 issuing the executive regulations for Law No. 8 of 2016 regarding the regulation of electronic media,
- Administrative Decision No. (122) of 2024 regarding the cancellation of Al-Kuwaitiya Newspaper <orig>الصحيفة الكويتية</orig> license,
- Administrative Decision No. 655 of 2022 regarding the delegation of certain competencies,
- Electronic media license No. 2016/40 issued on 29/11/2016,
- The letter from the Director of the Electronic Publishing Department No. 7 dated 16/1/2016.
- And as required by public interest.

**Has decided**

## Article One
License No. 2016/40 for the electronic media outlet "Al-Kuwaitiya Newspaper <orig>جريدة الكويتية</orig>" is hereby cancelled by operation of law, in accordance with Article (16), Clause 2 of Law No. 8 of 2016 regarding the regulation of electronic media.

## Article Two
Concerned parties shall be notified of this decision, and it shall be published on the Ministry's website and in the Official Gazette.

# Decision No. 1/11-R/2025

1- Amending the company's ownership structure to be:

8- The preliminary meeting and site inspection will be on Sunday, 3/2/2025, at 12:00 PM. 1.  The final deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on Thursday, 6/3/2025. No bids will be accepted after this time.
2.  Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Tenders and Follow-up Department <orig>إدارة المناقصات والمتابعة</orig> - Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> - Administrative Building - First Floor - Zone 7.
3.  Submission of an initial security deposit of not less than (2%) of the bid value, in favor of the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig>, in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check from one of the Kuwaiti banks <orig>البنوك الكويتية</orig>, valid throughout the bid validity period of (90) days.
4.  Submission of a valid national labor percentage fulfillment certificate.
5.  A letter of authorization and a copy of the civil ID for the company representative to purchase the auction document.
6.  This auction is indivisible, and alternative offers are not permitted.
7.  The bidder must submit a letter accompanied by a copy of the registration certificate with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
8.  The preliminary meeting and site inspection date is Sunday, 2/3/2025, at 12:00 PM. The bid must remain valid for (90) days from the closing date, with the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> reserving its right to extend or renew this period for such duration(s) as it deems appropriate to complete the award procedures.
9.  Must be registered in the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> Companies Register (Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> website).
    https://pnsd.da.gov.kw/ar
    The auction is subject to Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> Circular No. (1) of 2023 regarding auctions in public entities.
    For inquiries: Email: ad.alnassar@da.gov.kw - Direct: 22011424
    Undersecretary for Financial, Administrative, and Staff Affairs

# Correction Notice

The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces a material error in the advertisement published in Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> newspaper, Issue No. 1708, Seventieth Year, dated 10/13/2024, which stated the termination of the contractual relationship for a site lease contract for its preparation, development, and investment for artisanal and service purposes, an expansion of the Jahra <orig>الجهراء</orig> Craft Area <orig>المنطقة الحرفية بالجهراء</orig> site allocated to Agility Public Warehousing Company <orig>شركة اجيليتي للمخازن العمومية</orig> for utilization with an area of (44,000 m²), while the correct area is (244,000 m²).
Hence, this notice was necessary.

For inquiries: Email: ar.alduwailah@da.gov.kw
Direct: 22011438

Undersecretary for Financial, Administrative, and Staff Affairs
Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>

Announcement
Regarding the submission of Practice No. 1-2024/2025
Supply, installation, and maintenance of prosthetic devices (wheelchairs and hearing aids)
for the Public Authority for Persons with Disabilities <orig>الهيئة العامة لشئون ذوي الإعاقة</orig> for the fiscal year 2024/2025
Based on the request of the Public Authority for Persons with Disabilities <orig>الهيئة العامة لشئون ذوي الإعاقة</orig>
Practice documents can be obtained from the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.

<table_caption>Tender Details</table_caption>
<table>
| Submission Date | Deadline for Bid Submission (Closing Date) | Price | Guarantee |
|:------|:---|:------|:--------|
| 2025/02/02 | 2025/03/02 | 250 | Valid for 90 days in favor of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> |
| Preliminary Meeting (Inquiry Session) | At 10:00 AM on Sunday, 09-02-2025, at the headquarters of the Public Authority for Persons with Disabilities <orig>الهيئة العامة لشئون ذوي الإعاقة</orig>, Hawally Area <orig>منطقة حولي</orig> - Plot (11), Beirut Street <orig>شارع بيروت</orig> | | |
</table>

The practice documents will be published on the Agency's website for review before proceeding to purchase the documents. In the event of purchasing the documents and paying the prescribed fees, requests for fee refunds will not be accepted except in the case of cancellation of the practice in accordance with the provisions of Article (55) of the Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig>.
*   **The final time for submitting bids** is 1:00 PM on the day specified in the above announcement for bid submission.
*   **Bidders and practitioners must adhere to the instructions** regarding the submission and deposit of bids on the CD available on the Agency's website WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW.
*   **The cash equivalent** mentioned above shall be paid by certified check or K-Net card.
*   **Companies / bidders wishing to submit inquiries or clarifications** and other matters must adhere to submitting them to the concerned entity at the time and place specified above in the table for the preliminary meeting (inquiry session). No attention will be paid to any inquiries or clarifications submitted to the Agency.
*   **All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD**, except for the bid form and initial security, which must be submitted as hard copies.
*   **General practice** in accordance with the provisions of Article No. (17) of Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. (49) of 2016.
*   **Divisible**.
*   **Alternative offers are not accepted**.
*   **A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage**, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, must be submitted with the bid.
*   **The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate**, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, stating that there is no suspension on the bidder's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority due to one of the violations mentioned in Article 10 of Law No. 6 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. Bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.
*   **This announcement serves as an invitation for interested bidders to attend**, as interested companies have the right to attend the bid opening session.
*   **Interested companies wishing to attend must coordinate with the Bid Opening Department** before the specified date for the bid opening session and bring the following documents:-
    1.  Copy of the Civil ID.
    2.  Copy of the signature authorization for the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
    3.  In case of attendance by a person other than the authorized signatory, a written letter from the authorized signatory at the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> must be presented, authorizing the chosen representative to attend the session.
*   **Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises (SMEs)** are exempted from the prescribed fees for purchasing documents, in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. 49/2016.
*   **Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises (SMEs) wishing to apply for the tender** must attach with their bid a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for SME Care and Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig>, confirming their accreditation as a small or medium-sized enterprise.
*   **In accordance with the text of Article 48 of Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. 49 of 2016**, which stipulates:
    "Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the tender documents in a public session attended by bidders or their representatives."
*   **This announcement is considered an integral part of the tender documents.**
*   **For more information, please visit our website.** The Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> is valid with the submission of the bid.

Hence, this notice was necessary.

Central Agency for Public Tenders (CAPT) announces
the rebidding of Tender
(2021-2020/6)
Pertaining to Operation, Management, Training,
Maintenance Control & Oversight, Enhancement &
Services Development of Air Navigation Services at
Kuwait International Airport
The Central Agency for Public Tenders (CAPT) would like
to draw the attention of bidders, based on article (16) of
Law (49) dated 2016, to the rebidding of the tender
mentioned above and it will be open to the five (2) qualified
companies mentioned in the attached list after 30 days
.from the date of this announcement
Any interested party whose name is not listed has the right
to appeal within 30 days from the date of this
announcement in the official Gazette and after making the
payment stipulated in the Ministerial Resolution No
(2017/114)
Note: To view The criteria for qualification, refer to the
Electronic Website of the Central Agency for Public
Tenders (CAPT). (www.capt.gov.kw)

Held on the morning of (Tuesday)
28 Rajab 1446 AH - Corresponding to 28-01-2025 AD

at 9:00 AM on (Tuesday), 28-01-2025

## Announcement
The owners of the company / Nippon Al-Khadra Trading Company <orig>شركة نيبون الخضراء التجارية</orig> ## Company Under Liquidation
have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships at the Ministry to carry out/
Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company
Legal Entity:
One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership, only towards this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

request the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to proceed with / the dissolution and liquidation of the company.
Legal Entity:
Sole Proprietorship Company / One-Person Company <orig>شركة الشخص الواحد</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership <orig>شركة تضامنية</orig> or a simple limited partnership <orig>شركة توصية بسيطة</orig> only, towards this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on the objection.

## Announcement
### Tender Practice No. (2024-2025/17)
Related to the maintenance of precious metals management devices

The Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> announces the issuance of Tender Practice No. (2024-2025/17) for the benefit of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, in accordance with the general and special terms and specifications contained in the lists and documents of the practice available at the Ministry of Commerce and Industry. These can be obtained from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry - Financial Affairs Department <orig>إدارة الشؤون المالية</orig> - Procurement and Stores Control <orig>مراقبة المشتريات والمخازن</orig> - Tenders and Contracts Section <orig>قسم المناقصات والعقود</orig> - Ministries Complex, Block No. (1), Third Floor, Room No. (1307). A non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> per copy is required, payable via K-NET, during official working hours.
Bids shall be submitted to the Procurement and Stores Control <orig>مراقبة المشتريات والمخازن</orig> by 12:00 PM on Monday, 17/02/2025. These bids shall be valid for ninety days from the date of opening the envelopes, provided that the submitted price is final.
The value of the preliminary guarantee for this bid shall not be less than (2%) of the bid value and must be valid throughout the bid's validity period.

Undersecretary of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وكيل وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>

### Monday, 16 December 2024

Mohammed Adel Al-Waqyan <orig>محمد عادل الوقيان</orig>, representative of Gulf Securities Depository Company <orig>الشركة الخليجية لحفظ الأوراق المالية</orig>.
5. Mohammed Zakaria Awad <orig>محمد زكريا عوض</orig>, Board Secretary.
6. And shareholders holding 148,048 original shares, equivalent to (1.5087%), and 6,689,944 proxy shares, equivalent to (68.1749%), totaling 6,837,992 shares, equivalent to (69.6836%), noting that the paid-up capital is 981,291 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig>.
After the announcement of the legal quorum for the deferred Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية المؤجلة</orig>.
Ms. Intisar Abdulrahim Al-Suwaidi <orig>انتصار عبدالرحيم السويدي</orig>, Chairperson of the Board of Directors (Chairperson of the Assembly), opened the meeting by welcoming the attendees. The items on the agenda were discussed, and the deferred Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية المؤجلة</orig> approved the following resolutions:
1) Approval was granted to increase the authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital from KWD 981,291 (Nine Hundred Eighty-One Thousand Two Hundred Ninety-One Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) to KWD 1,000,000 (One Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) by settling part of the debt owed to Ms. Intisar Abdulrahim Al-Suwaidi <orig>انتصار عبدالرحيم السويدي</orig> in the amount of KWD 18,709 (Eighteen Thousand Seven Hundred Nine Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) through the issuance of 187,090 new shares (One Hundred Eighty-Seven Thousand Ninety Shares) at a nominal value of (100 fils) per share, in her favor against that debt, with shareholders waiving their right to the increase.
*   Shareholders owning 13.526% of the capital did not approve or had reservations about the item.
*   Baytack Capital Investment Company <orig>شركة بيتك كابيتال للاستثمار</orig>, which owns 6.609% of the capital.
*   Kuwaiti Industrial Projects Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمشروعات الصناعية</orig>, which owns 6.917% of the capital.
2) Approval was granted to amend Article (6) of the Articles of Incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and Article (5) of the Company's Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig> as follows:

<table_caption>Comparison of Company Capital Before and After Amendment</table_caption>
<table>
| Text Before Amendment | Text After Amendment |
|:---|:---|
| The authorized, issued, and paid-up capital of the company was set at KWD 981,291 (Nine Hundred Eighty-One Thousand Two Hundred Ninety-One Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), distributed over 9,812,910 shares (Nine Million Eight Hundred Twelve Thousand Nine Hundred Ten Shares), with a value of 100 fils per share, and all shares are cash shares. | The authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital of the company was set at KWD 1,000,000 (One Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), distributed over 10,000,000 shares (Ten Million Shares), with a value of 100 fils per share, and all shares are cash shares. |
</table>

*   Shareholders owning 13.526% of the capital did not approve or had reservations about the item.
*   Baytack Capital Investment Company <orig>شركة بيتك كابيتال للاستثمار</orig>, which owns 6.609% of the capital.
*   Kuwaiti Industrial Projects Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمشروعات الصناعية</orig>, which owns 6.917% of the capital.
3) Approval was granted to regularize the company's activities according to the international classification and to amend Article (5) of the Articles of Incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and Article (4) of the Company's Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig> as follows:

### Text Before Amendment
The purposes for which the company was established are to carry out the following:
1.  Development of computer systems and software, and localization systems for computer devices and their accessories.
2.  Development of communication systems and software, and utilization of specialized technical labor.
3.  Sale, purchase, rental, installation, and design of computer systems and software, and eligibility applications.
4.  Training governmental bodies, institutions, individuals, and companies on integrated systems, e-commerce, e-government, and website design.
5.  Building and operating computer communication networks connected to databases, call centers, and customer service, and leasing them inside and outside the building.
6.  Designing and equipping electronic computer centers and information systems for the company and third parties.
7.  Marketing and maintenance of electronic safety and security systems, and providing connectivity services, electronic messaging services, and electronic information banks.
8.  Manufacturing, production, and operation of smart electronic cards to cover demand in the field of communication and pre-payment equipment, as well as for communication uses and their wholesale spare parts.
9.  Managing and operating card-related data on behalf of clients, as well as data related to sales operations.
10. Sale of computers and peripheral equipment.
11. Wired telecommunications activities.
12. Wireless telecommunications activities.
13. Computer dealer.

### Text After Amendment

The Board of Directors shall have the broadest powers to manage the company and perform all acts required for the company's management in accordance with its objectives, and this authority shall not be limited by

# Al-Kawn Computer Company K.S.C.C. <orig>شركة الكون للكمبيوتر ش.م.ك.م.</orig> (Under Liquidation)
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting (Adjourned)
### Held on 27/1/2025

On Monday, 27/1/2025, at 11:30 AM, the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting (Adjourned) of the shareholders of Al-Kawn Computer Company K.S.C.C. <orig>شركة الكون للكمبيوتر ش.م.ك.م.</orig> (Under Liquidation) was held at the office of the company's liquidator, located in (Al-Qibla <orig>القبلة</orig> - Ali Al-Salem Street <orig>شارع علي السالم</orig> - Al-Thuwaini Building <orig>عمارة الثويني</orig> - Third Floor).
Mr. Barrak Abdul Hassan Al-Otaiqi <orig>براك عبد الحسن العتيقي</orig> chaired the meeting session in his capacity as the liquidator of Al-Kawn Computer Company K.S.C.C. <orig>شركة الكون للكمبيوتر ش.م.ك.م.</orig>
Shareholders holding 14,000,000 shares, in person and by proxy, representing 70% of the capital shares, which number 20,000,000 shares, were present.
Mr. Barrak Abdul Hassan Al-Otaiqi <orig>براك عبد الحسن العتيقي</orig> opened the meeting and announced the completion of the legal quorum for the validity of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting (Adjourned). He then proceeded to discuss the item mentioned in the agenda of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting (Adjourned). The Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting (Adjourned) approved the item mentioned in the agenda with 100% consensus of those present, as follows:
1.  The extension of the liquidation period for Mr. Barrak Abdul Hassan Al-Otaiqi <orig>براك عبدالحسن العتيقي</orig> to complete the liquidation work for a period of one year was approved.
At the conclusion of the meeting, Mr. Barrak Abdul Hassan Al-Otaiqi <orig>براك عبد الحسن العتيقي</orig> - Chairman of the meeting - thanked the attendees, and the proceedings of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting (Adjourned) concluded at 11:45 AM.

The Liquidator

---

# Al-Ahliya Electrical Panels Company <orig>الشركة الأهلية للوحات الكهرباء</orig>
(K.S.C.C.)
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting

On Thursday, 23/1/2025, at 10:30 AM, in Al-Qibla <orig>القبلة</orig> area - Plot 2 - Block No. 5 - Office No. 114, the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting of the company commenced as follows:
1- Shareholders representing 100% of the company's capital, amounting to K.D. 30,000,000, were present.
2- Mr. Ma'moun Mousa Al-Mabrouk <orig>مأمون موسى المبروك</orig> - Secretary of the Board of Directors - was present.
The session opened at 10:30 AM to discuss the agenda, a copy of which was distributed to each attendee. The attendees resolved the following:-
- The amendment of the text of Article No. (5) of the Articles of Association and Article No. (4) of the Company's Memorandum of Association was approved to align the company's activities with the International Standard Industrial Classification of All Economic Activities (ISIC) regarding the company's objectives, as follows:
The objectives for which the company is established are as follows:
1) Design, manufacture, and marketing of low-voltage electrical switchgear distribution panels.
2) Trading in all electrical supplies necessary to achieve the company's objectives, including their import and export.
3) Electrical contracting.
4) Representing similar foreign factories and companies in Kuwait and the Middle East. The company may have an interest in or participate in any way with entities that engage in similar activities or that may assist it in achieving its objectives in Kuwait and abroad. It may acquire or merge with such entities after obtaining collective approval from the General Assembly.
5) Utilizing the company's available financial surpluses by investing them in financial portfolios managed by specialized companies and entities.
6) Production of medium-voltage electrical switchgear distribution panels.
7) Production of high-voltage panels.
8) Production of battery charging panels.
9) Production of electrical current transformers used in electrical panels.
10) Production of voltage transformers (power distribution).
11) Production of electrical insulating panels and circuit breakers, and electrical industries.
12) Production of substations (integrated plans).
13) Import of chemical materials solely for the company's purposes.
Text of the Article after Amendment:
The objectives for which the company was established are as follows:
1) Manufacture of integrated circuits (261004).
2) Manufacture of power transformers for electronic uses (261005).
3) Manufacture of electric motors, generators, transformers, and electricity distribution and control apparatus (271000).
4) Manufacture of electrical transformers (271020).
5) Manufacture of electricity distribution and control apparatus (271030).
6) Rewinding of magnetic cores for electric generators, motors, and transformers (271040).
7) Manufacture of parts for electric generators, motors, and power transformers (271050).
<page_end>52</page_end>

# Ministry of Education / Wizarat Al-Tarbiya <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>
## Announcement of Lost Certificate
Based on Ministerial Resolution No. (2000/89) issued on 6/13/2000 AD regarding the issuance of a replacement certificate (for a lost one).
The Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig> announces that student / Ali Jabara Mohammed Refaat Abu Jabara <orig>علي جباره محمد رفعت أبو جباره</orig>, from Al-Wataniya Al-Ahliya Secondary School for Boys <orig>المدرسة الوطنية الأهلية الثانوية للبنين المشتركة</orig>, has lost his original certificate, and a replacement certificate (for a lost one) is being issued for him after publication in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>).
Undersecretary of the Ministry of Education / Wizarat Al-Tarbiya <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Announcements from the Ministry of Interior and Ministry of Foreign Affairs <orig>إعلانات وزارة الداخلية ووزارة الخارجية</orig>",

  "page_summary": "This page contains two official announcements: one from the Ministry of Interior regarding lost Kuwaiti nationality certificates and travel documents, and another from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs announcing a tender for the comprehensive operation and maintenance of the NATO building and National Security building in Mishref."

</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
56
</header>
Ref: 14 / 2024-2025 Comprehensive Operation and Maintenance of the NATO <orig>حلف الشمال الأطلسي</orig> Building and the National Security <orig>الأمن الوطني</orig> Building in Mishref <orig>مشرف</orig>

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs <orig>وزارة الخارجية</orig> announces its need to issue a practice for the comprehensive operation and maintenance of the NATO <orig>حلف الشمال الأطلسي</orig> Building and the National Security <orig>الأمن الوطني</orig> Building in Mishref <orig>مشرف</orig>, according to the general and special conditions and technical specifications outlined in the practice documents. Specialized companies wishing to participate in the practice are kindly requested to review the Procurement and Custody Control Department at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs <orig>وزارة الخارجية</orig> building - Arabian Gulf Street <orig>شارع الخليج العربي</orig>, to obtain the practice documents during official working hours from (10:00 AM) until (1:00 PM) for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> in cash. The practice documents must be purchased during the period from Sunday, 2/2/2025, until Thursday, 2/20/2025, with the inclusion of the following documents:

1- An authorization letter from the company to purchase the practice documents in the name of the individual, along with a copy of their civil ID.
2- Payment of the prescribed fees for purchasing the practice documents.
3- A copy of the commercial register.
4- A recent copy of the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة الكويت</orig> certificate.
5- A recent copy of the registration receipt with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
6- The company must be specialized in this field.
7- Annual employment percentage certificate.

In addition to any other conditions deemed appropriate by the competent authority, please note that the preliminary meeting for the practice will be held on Monday, 2/10/2025, at 11:00 AM at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs <orig>وزارة الخارجية</orig> building - Arabian Gulf Street <orig>شارع الخليج العربي</orig>. The deadline for submitting bids and closing is Thursday, 2/20/2025, from 10:00 AM until 1:00 PM. No bids submitted before or after this deadline will be accepted.

Bids shall be valid for a period of (90) ninety days from the date of bid opening. The value of the preliminary guarantee is (2500) Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, and it must be valid throughout the bid validity period (note that the practice is indivisible).

For inquiries, please contact Mr. Mohammed Abathra'a <orig>محمد اباذراع</orig> at 7731 - or Ms. Sabika Al-Saddani <orig>سبيكة السداني</orig> at Tel: 22225555 - Ext: 1128.

# Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>

(P. 2024/35-2025) Repair, operation, and maintenance of various security systems and spare parts for different departments within the Ministry. For the General Department of Security Systems <orig>الإدارة العامة للأنظمة الأمنية</orig>.

Therefore, companies / establishments specialized in this field should refer to the General Department of Financial Affairs <orig>الإدارة العامة للشئون المالية</orig> - Tenders Department <orig>إدارة المناقصات</orig> (in Al-Ardiya Industrial Area <orig>بالعارضية الصناعية</orig>) to obtain the documents for this practice for a fee of (150/-) K.D. (one hundred and fifty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> only) (via K-Net) (non-refundable). An initial guarantee of (5,000/-) K.D. for a period of (90 days) must be submitted (to be attached with the bid submitted in the practice), noting that the final insurance for the practice is (10%) of the total contract value. They must bring a copy of the practice announcement in the Official Gazette (Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>), and the following documents:

- Valid registration receipt from the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>. Or
- A registration request for registration with the Ministry and then purchasing the practice documents. Please note that the closing date (submission of bids) is Wednesday, 26/3/2025, from (10:00) ten AM until (1:00) one PM. No bids submitted before or after the mentioned time will be accepted. Bids must be submitted in sealed envelopes at the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> building (Sharq Area <orig>منطقة شرق</orig> – Al-Siddiq School <orig>مدرسة الصديق</orig> – First Floor).

Two mandatory preliminary meetings will be held to answer inquiries from companies participating in the practice: the first on Wednesday, 12/2/2025, at (10:00) AM, and the second on Tuesday, 11/3/2025, at (11:00) AM, at the headquarters of the General Department of Security Systems <orig>الإدارة العامة للأنظمة الأمنية</orig>. Please note that any recommendations or decisions resulting from these meetings are an integral part of the practice documents and are binding on all companies, whether the participant attended the mandatory preliminary meetings or not.

(three hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only) (via K-Net). A preliminary guarantee of (15,000/-) K.D. (fifteen thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only) must be submitted and specified in the financial bid for the practice. # Announcement

## Ministry of Defense <orig>وزارة الدفاع</orig>
# Announcement

The Ministry of Defense <orig>وزارة الدفاع</orig> announces the issuance of Tender No. (1482724) specific to the Ministry of Defense. Tender documents can be obtained from the Military Installations Engineering Department <orig>هندسة المنشآت العسكرية</orig> (Tenders Control - Maidan Hawally <orig>ميدان حولي</orig>).

<table_caption>Tender Details for Ministry of Defense (Tender No. 1482724)</table_caption>
<table>
| Issue | Closing | Price | Initial Guarantee |
|:------|:--------|:------|:---|
| 2025-02-02 | 2025-03-18 | 75 K.D. | 2000 K.D. valid for 90 days |
</table>

*   **Site Visit**
    At 9:00 AM on Tuesday, 11/02/2025, at the headquarters of the Military Installations Engineering Department <orig>هندسة المنشآت العسكرية</orig> - Maidan Hawally <orig>ميدان حولي</orig>.
*   **Preliminary Meeting**
    At 10:00 AM on Wednesday, 12/02/2025, at the headquarters of the Military Installations Engineering Department <orig>هندسة المنشآت العسكرية</orig> - Maidan Hawally <orig>ميدان حولي</orig>.
*   **Instructions**
    1- The Ministry must be notified of the names, positions, and passports of candidates attending the site visit seven days prior to the date. Fax submissions will not be accepted.
    2- The tender purchase receipt must be presented when attending the site visit and the preliminary meeting.
    3- An authorization letter for purchasing tender documents.
    4- A certificate of national labor percentage must be submitted with the bid.
    5- The last deadline for purchasing tender documents is 1:00 PM on Sunday, 09-03-2025.
    6- The last deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM at the Mail and Tenders Delivery Center (Window No. 1 – Box No. 3 – Committee for Military Material Purchases and Military Installations Contracts Below Legal Threshold) next to Gate No. 12, beside the Military Sports Federation <orig>الاتحاد العسكري الرياضي</orig>.
    7- This tender is general for companies specialized in the field of supplying construction materials, fulfilling all conditions stated in the tender documents, and registered with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.

Companies wishing to participate must adhere to the following:
1.  Submission of a copy of the registration card with the Ministry of Defense <orig>وزارة الدفاع</orig> / Local Supply Department <orig>إدارة التجهيز المحلي</orig> for the year 2025.
2.  Submission of an authorization letter from the company to purchase the documents.
3.  The company must be specialized in this field and classified by the Ministry's Companies Classification Control <orig>مراقبة تصنيف الشركات</orig>.
4.  Submission of a copy of the national labor support certificate for non-governmental companies (annual).
5.  Submission of an official letter for any inquiries within (one week) from the date of publication of the announcement.
6.  Payment of the prescribed fees for purchasing practice documents via (K. NET).

among companies in accordance with the general and special conditions outlined in the tender documents, which can be obtained from the Ministry's website (www.moh.gov.kw) upon payment of a non-refundable fee (as per the booklet prices indicated in the table above).

Announcement
We are pleased to invite you to collect Addendum No. (1) for Practice No. P/M/97/2024/2025, concerning the completion of remaining works for the construction, completion, and maintenance of the Farwaniya Specialized Health Clinic <orig>مستوصف الفروانية الصحي التخصصي</orig> building, executed at the expense of the contractor for Contract No. P/M.Kh.A/26/2014/2015 – 114, in accordance with the conditions specified in the practice documents, taking into account the following:
1- This practice is restricted to companies classified in categories one and two in the field of construction works by the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
2- It is necessary to visit the Ministry to collect Addendum No. (1) for the practice at the Financial Affairs Department <orig>جهاز الشئون المالية</orig> – First Floor – Procurement Department <orig>إدارة المشتريات</orig> – Ministry Building in Sulaibikhat <orig>الصليبيخات</orig> during official working hours.
3- Submission of a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file regarding government contracts submitted to the Authority. Please note that bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.
4- Submission of an initial guarantee (letter of guarantee or certified check) amounting to K.D. 50,000.000 (fifty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars only), valid throughout the bid's validity period.
5- The cost of the documents can be paid via the online service through the Ministry's website (www.moh.gov.kw) for an amount of K.D. 1,000.000 (one thousand Kuwaiti Dinars only) or via K-Net at the Treasury Department <orig>قسم الخزينة</orig> – Financial Department <orig>إدارة المالية</orig>.
6- All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, with the exception of the bid form and initial insurance, which must be submitted as hard copies.
7- The practice is indivisible.
8- The final deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on Monday, 17/02/2025, at the tenders box in the Procurement Department <orig>إدارة المشتريات</orig>. Bids are valid for a period of (90) days from the closing date.
9- This announcement and the addendum are considered an integral part of the practice documents. The practitioner must submit this addendum after signing it and stamping each page with the company's or institution's seal, attaching it with the practice documents.

# Announcement

The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> - Medical Supplies Control <orig>مراقبة اللوازم الطبية</orig>) announces the offering of the following practice:

<table_caption>Medical Practice Details for Cardiac Surgery Departments</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Practice No. | Description | Fees | Closing Date |
|:--|:---|:---|:-------|:---|
| 1 | 4CC015 | Surgical kits for adult cardiac surgery departments in hospitals | 1000 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the tender box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids shall be valid for (90) days from the closing date.

The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the practice:

1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field and be documented with an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical and Herbal Drugs <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنباتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers' register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> within the contents of the submitted bid (specific to drug control).
5- Submit samples of new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, to the competent control (drugs - medical supplies).
6- Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7- Practice documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
8- The booklet purchase fees can be paid from the website to be attached with the practice documents.
9- Submit price offers in a sealed envelope, including the practice documents, according to the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724, Seventy-First Year
65
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
</header>

Companies wishing to participate in the practice must meet the following conditions:
1.  The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
2.  The local company must specialize in the medical field and be certified by an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3.  When submitting two offers, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
4.  Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical and Herbal Drugs <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنباتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers' register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> within the contents of the submitted tender (specific to drug control).
5.  Provide samples of new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for accredited control (drugs - medical supplies).
6.  Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7.  Practice documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
8.  The fees for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the practice documents.
9.  Submit price offers in a sealed envelope, including practice documents, according to the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.

Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> – Medical Supplies Control <orig>مراقبة اللوازم الطبية</orig>) announces the following practices:

<table_caption>Tenders from the Ministry of Health (Medical Warehouses Department - Medical Supplies Control)</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Practice No. | Description | Fees | Closing Date |
|:----|:---|:------|:------|:---|
| 1   | 5EN008      | Consumables for ENT operations for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 75    | 10 days from announcement date or more |
| 2   | 5EN009      | Consumables for ENT operations for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 75    | 10 days from announcement date or more |
| 3   | 5EY005      | Consumables for eye operations for the needs of the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> | 75    | 10 days from announcement date or more |
| 4   | 5RZF03      | Special knee joint surgery consumables for the needs of Al-Farwaniya Hospital <orig>مستشفى الفروانية</orig> | 75    | 10 days from announcement date or more |
| 5   | 5RZF05      | Special knee joint surgery consumables for the needs of Al-Farwaniya Hospital <orig>مستشفى الفروانية</orig> | 75    | 10 days from announcement date or more |
| 6   | 5DS010      | Consumables for general surgery and general and specialized surgery departments for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 75    | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 7   | 5SSJ02      | Consumables for neurosurgery for the needs of Jaber Al-Ahmad Hospital <orig>مستشفى جابر الأحمد</orig> | 75    | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 8   | 5RZF02      | Consumables used in orthopedic arthroscopic surgery for the needs of Al-Farwaniya Hospital <orig>مستشفى الفروانية</orig> | 75    | 30 days from announcement date or more |
| 9   | 5RZF06      | Special knee and hip joint surgery consumables for the needs of Al-Farwaniya Hospital <orig>مستشفى الفروانية</orig> | 75    | 30 days from announcement date or more |
| 10  | 5RZF07      | Screws and plates used for hand surgeries for the needs of Al-Farwaniya Hospital <orig>مستشفى الفروانية</orig> | 75    | 30 days from announcement date or more |
</table>

Tenders shall be placed in the tender box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and the tenders must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
Companies wishing to participate in the practice must meet the following conditions:
1.  The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
2.  The local company must specialize in the medical field and be certified by an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3.  When submitting two offers, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.

-4 Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Drug and Botanical Registration and Control <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية والنباتية</orig> or proof of certificate submission, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> as part of the bid contents (specific to Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>).

## Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> - Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>) announces the offering of the following practices:

<table_caption>Tenders for Drug Control Practices from the Ministry of Health</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Practice No. | Description | Fees | Closing Date |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | 5IN012 | Medications (injections) for treating fungi, needed by all hospitals | 75 | 10 days from announcement date or more |
| 2 | 5TB020 | (Pills) for immune activation, needed by all departments in specialized centers and hospitals | 75 | 10 days from announcement date or more |
| 3 | 5TB017 | (Pills) for treating bariatric surgery patients, needed by all hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 4 | 5TB021 | (Pills) for treating psychiatric illnesses, needed by all departments in specialized centers and hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 5 | 5NU001 | Therapeutic nutritional substance, needed by all hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 6 | 5SP012 | (Granules) antibiotic, needed by all hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 7 | 5TB022 | (Pills) for treating heart diseases, needed by all hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 8 | 5IN007 | (Injections) for treating hemorrhage, needed by all hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the bids box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and the bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the practice:
-1 The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers register.
-2 The local company must specialize in the medical field and be documented with an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
-3 When submitting an offer, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
-4 Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Drug and Botanical Registration and Control <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية والنباتية</orig> or proof of certificate submission, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> as part of the bid contents (specific to Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>).

## Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> - Medical Supplies Control <orig>مراقبة اللوازم الطبية</orig>) announces the offering of the following practices:

<table_caption>Tenders for Medical Supplies Control Practices from the Ministry of Health</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Practice No. | Description | Fees | Closing Date |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | 4SRB14 | Supplies for surgery, needed by Jaber Al-Ahmad Hospital <orig>مستشفى جابر الأحمد</orig> | 75 | 10 days from announcement date |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the bids box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and the bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the practice:
-1 The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers register.
-2 The local company must specialize in the medical field and be documented with an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
-3 When submitting an offer, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
-4 Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Drug and Botanical Registration and Control <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية والنباتية</orig> or proof of certificate submission, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> as part of the bid contents (specific to Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>).
-5 Submission of samples for new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for specialized control (Drugs <orig>الأدوية</orig> – Medical Supplies <orig>اللوازم الطبية</orig>).
-6 Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
-7 Practice documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
-8 The fees for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the practice documents.
-9 Submission of price offers in a sealed envelope, inclusive with the practice documents, according to the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
