# Announcement

The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> – Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>) announces the offering of the following practices:

<table_caption>Tenders for Medical Supplies and Services (Part 1)</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Practice No. | Description | Fees | Closing Date |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | 5TB023 | (Pills) for the treatment of psychiatric illnesses for the needs of all hospitals | 75 | 10 days from announcement date or more |
| 2 | 5ON001 | Injections for the treatment of cancer patients for the needs of Hussein Makki Juma Center <orig>مركز حسين مكي جمعة</orig> for Specialized Surgeries | 75 | 10 days from announcement date or more |
| 3 | 5ON003 | Injections for the treatment of cancer patients for the needs of all hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 4 | 5TB015 | (Capsules) for the treatment of psychiatric illnesses for the needs of all hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 5 | 5TB018 | (Pills) for the treatment of fungal infections for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 6 | 4LQ132 | Chemicals for pharmaceutical preparations for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 7 | 5SP017 | Vaccine for the treatment of heart diseases for the needs of all hospitals | 75 | 20 days from announcement date or more |
| 8 | 5VA003 | Human anti-toxin immunoglobulin for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 75 | 30 days from announcement date or more |
| 9 | 5SP011 | Gel for the treatment of oral fungal infections for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 75 | 30 days from announcement date or more |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the bid box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, provided that
The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the practice:
-1 The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
-2 The local company must specialize in the medical field and be documented with a certified certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
-3 When submitting an offer, two booklets must be purchased with two different receipts.
-4 Attachment of a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Drug and Herbal Registration and Control <orig>إدارة تسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية والنباتية</orig> or proof of submission of the certificate and a copy of the manufacturer's registration and extension in the suppliers' register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> within the contents of the submitted bid (specific to Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>).
-5 Submission of samples for new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for specialized control (drugs – medical supplies).
-6 Attachment of a national labor support ratio certificate.
-7 Practice documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> website.
-8 The booklet purchase fees can be paid from the website to be attached with the practice documents.
-9 Submission of price offers in a sealed envelope, including the practice documents, according to the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> website.

## Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> - Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>) announces the offering of the following practices:

<table_caption>Tender Details for Medical Supplies (First Announcement)</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Practice No. | Description | Fees | Closing Date |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | 4TB091 | (Pills) for the treatment of neurological diseases for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 150 | 20 days from the date of announcement or more |
| 2 | 4TB417 | (Pills) for the treatment of psychiatric diseases for the needs of all departments in specialized centers and hospitals | 150 | 20 days from the date of announcement or more |
| 3 | 4TB426 | (Pills) for the treatment of diabetes for the needs of all hospitals | 150 | 20 days from the date of announcement or more |
| 4 | 4TB427 | (Pills) for the treatment of pulmonary hypertension for the needs of all hospitals | 1000 | 20 days from the date of announcement or more |
| 5 | 4IN407 | Dye injections for all hospitals | 1000 | 20 days from the date of announcement or more |
| 6 | 4VA025 | (Pills) for the treatment of blood diseases for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 150 | 30 days from the date of announcement or more |
| 7 | 4IN428 | Medications (pills) for the treatment of blood thinning for the needs of all hospitals | 1000 | 30 days from the date of announcement or more |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the bid box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
Companies wishing to participate in the practice must meet the following conditions:
1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field and be documented with an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Registration and Drug and Herbal Control Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية والنباتية</orig> or proof of submission of the certificate and a copy of the registration
of the manufacturing company and the material in the suppliers' register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> within the contents of the submitted bid (specific to Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>).
5- Submission of samples for new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturing company, to the competent control (Drugs - Medical Supplies).
6- Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7- Practice documents can be obtained from the official website of the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>.
8- The fees for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the practice documents.
9- Price offers must be submitted in a sealed envelope, including the practice documents, according to the closing date specified on the official website of the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>.

The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the practice/tender:
1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field and be certified by an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Drug and Herbal Control <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية والنباتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers' register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> as part of the tender contents (specific to drug control).
5- Submit samples of new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for the specialized control (drugs – medical supplies).
6- Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7- Practice/tender documents can be obtained from the official website of the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>.
8- The fee for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the practice/tender documents.
9- Submit price offers in a sealed envelope, including the practice/tender documents, according to the closing date specified on the official website of the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>.

## Announcement

<table_caption>Tender Details for Medical Store Management</table_caption>
<table>

|:--------------------|:-------------------------------------------------------------------------|:-----|:---------------------------------|

The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> - Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>) announces the launch of the following practices/tenders:
Bids shall be placed in the tender box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the practice/tender:
1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field and be certified by an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Drug and Herbal Control <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية والنباتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers' register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> as part of the tender contents (specific to drug control).
5- Submit samples of new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for the specialized control (drugs – medical supplies).
6- Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7- Practice/tender documents can be obtained from the official website of the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>.
8- The fee for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the practice/tender documents.
9- Submit price offers in a sealed envelope, including the practice/tender documents, according to the closing date specified on the official website of the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>.

<table_caption>Tender Details for Drug Control (Ministry of Health)</table_caption>
<table>
| Practice/Tender No. | Description                                                              | Fees | Closing Date                     |
|:--------------------|:-------------------------------------------------------------------------|:-----|:---------------------------------|
| 4TB410              | (Pills) for the treatment of viral hepatitis (C) patients, especially all hospitals | 1000 | 10 days from the announcement date or more |
| 4TB415              | (Pills) for the treatment of thalassemia patients, especially all hospitals | 1000 | 30 days from the announcement date or more |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the tender box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the practice/tender:
1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
<page_end>69</page_end>

## Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>
Held on 2025/01/07

After reviewing the requests submitted for amending data in the birth and death records, it was decided to make the amendment listed below in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> (Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>). If the committee does not receive any objection within fifteen days from the date of publication of this announcement, the amendment will be made in the records, and birth or death certificates will be issued according to the following amendment:

## Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>
Held on 2025/01/07
The Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>, stipulated in Article 15 of Law No. 69/36 and formed by Ministerial Resolution No. 2021/1650, met.
*   Mr. / Director of the Central Registry Department for Births and Deaths <orig>مدير إدارة السجل المركزي للمواليد والوفيات</orig>
*   Mr. / Head of Research and Opinion Section <orig>رئيس قسم البحوث والرأي</orig>
*   Mr. / Head of Deaths Section <orig>رئيس قسم الوفيات</orig>
*   Mr. / Head of Records Section <orig>رئيس قسم السجلات</orig>
*   Ms. / Shukriya Al-Duraie <orig>شكرية الدريعي</orig> acted as the Committee Secretary.

Chairman: Dr. / Head of the General Medical Council <orig>رئيس المجلس الطبي العام</orig>
Member: Mr. / Head of Registration Section <orig>رئيس قسم القيد</orig>
Member: Mr. / Legal Researcher <orig>الباحث القانوني</orig>
Member:

The Committee reviewed requests from number ((01)) to number ((17)) in the attached list concerning the amendment of data in birth and death records, with requests for birth and death registration approvals. After its review and verification of the completeness of documents and papers, the Committee decided to announce the amendments and requests in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> (Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) in two consecutive issues. If the legal period (fifteen days) from the date of the last announcement expires and no one submits any other objections, the amendments will be made in the registers, and birth and death certificates will be issued.

Head of Records Section <orig>رئيس قسم السجلات</orig>

## Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig> in its Session No. 02 for the year 2025 held on 14/01/2025

After reviewing the requests submitted for amending data in the birth and death records, the Committee, in its meeting held on 14/01/2025, Session No. 02 for the year 2025, decided that if no objection is received within fifteen days from the date of publication of this announcement, the amendment will be made in the records, and birth or death certificates will be issued according to the following amendment:

## Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig> in its Session held on 14/01/2025, No. 02 for the year 2025

The Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>, stipulated in Article 15 of Law No. 36/1969 and formed by Ministerial Resolution No. 1650/2021, met.

- Mr. / Director of the Central Registry Department for Births and Deaths <orig>إدارة السجل المركزي للمواليد والوفيات</orig>: Chairman
- Dr. / Head of the General Medical Council <orig>المجلس الطبي العام</orig>: Member

- Mr. / Head of the Deaths Section <orig>قسم الوفيات</orig>: Member
- Mr. / Head of the Records Section <orig>قسم السجلات</orig>: Member
- Mr. / Legal Researcher <orig>الباحث القانوني</orig>: Member

Ms. / Alia Al-Saffar <orig>علياء الصفار</orig> acted as the Committee's secretary.

The Committee reviewed requests from No. (18) to No. (30) in the attached list concerning the amendment of data in birth and death records for unregistered birth and death applications. After reviewing and ensuring the completeness of documents and supporting papers, the Committee decided to announce the amendments and requests in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) in two consecutive issues. If the legal period (fifteen days) from the date of the last announcement expires and no objection is submitted, the amendments will be made in the registers, and birth and death certificates will be issued.

## Announcement of Public Auction for Cars

The General Department of Execution <orig>الإدارة العامة للتنفيذ</orig> announces that on Wednesday, 5/2/2025, and the following three days, starting from 8:00 AM, the following cars will be sold by public auction at the Sales Seizure Garage <orig>كراج حجز البيوع</orig>, in implementation of judgments. Please note that the sale procedures will take place at the Sales Center <orig>مركز البيوع</orig> – Al-Ardiya Industrial Area <orig>العارضية الحرفية</orig>. Note: Full payment via K-Net <orig>الكي نت</orig> on the same day.

Please note that vehicle inspection will be at Doha Seizure Yard <orig>محجز الدوحة</orig> on Tuesday and Wednesday from 8:00 AM to 1:00 PM, and the sale will take place at the Sales Center <orig>مركز البيوع</orig> in Al-Ardiya Industrial Area <orig>العارضية الحرفية</orig> at 3:30 PM.

## Announcement of Sale of Seized Items by Public Auction
The Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig> - Capital Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة تنفيذ العاصمة</orig> announces that on Wednesday, 5/2/2025 AD, starting from 11:00 AM, seized items will be sold by public auction, located in Shuwaikh Industrial Area <orig>الشويخ الصناعية</orig> - Block 3B - Street 49 - Plot 100 - Solution No. 14 - Automated Address Number (20631117). The seized items are owned by the defendant / GM Clean Station Company for Building Cleaning Contracting <orig>شركة جي ام كلين ستيشن لمقاولات تنظيف المباني</orig>, and are detailed in the executive seizure report dated 27/11/2022, file No. 220472810. These items were seized after complete evacuation in favor of the seizer / Khalid Ali Al-Kharafi and Brothers Construction Contracting Company <orig>شركة خالد علي الخرافي وإخوانه للمقاولات الإنشائية</orig> - in fulfillment of an amount of (12,898.700) K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>.
Those wishing to purchase must attend at the time and place specified above. Anyone wishing to view further details should refer to the Compulsory Enforcement Section <orig>قسم التنفيذ الجبري</orig> - Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> during official working hours. For clarification, we announce.
Head of Capital Enforcement Department <orig>رئيس إدارة تنفيذ العاصمة</orig>

## Committee for Lineage Claims and Name Correction <orig>لجنة دعاوى النسب وتصحيح الأسماء</orig>

### Al-Tamdeen International Hotels Company <orig>شركة التمدين العالمية للفنادق</orig>
Kuwaiti Closed Shareholding Company (K.C.S.C.)
Articles of Association

On this day: Sunday, corresponding to: **26/01/2025** AD
Before me: **Sundus Khudair Dahal Al-Anzi <orig>سندس خضير دحل العنزي</orig>**, Notary Public at the Department:
Appeared before me each of:

**First Party / Founder**
Al-Tamdeen Investment Company <orig>شركه التمدين الاستثمارية</orig>, a Kuwaiti Public Shareholding Company, of Kuwaiti nationality
Card No. **1477189**
Whose Articles of Association were notarized under No. **359**, Volume **1**, dated **03/03/1997**, and represented by
Mr. **Mohammed Mustafa Marzouq Al-Marzouq <orig>محمد مصطفى مرزوق المرزوق</orig>** – of Kuwaiti nationality –
holding Civil ID No. (**279103100013**) in his capacity as the Chief Executive Officer of the company, pursuant to a certificate of incumbency issued by the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> dated **18/07/2024**.

**Second Party / Founder**
Wafra Holding Company <orig>شركه وفره القابضة</orig> – a Kuwaiti Closed Shareholding Company, of Kuwaiti nationality
Card No. **2514739**
Whose Articles of Association were notarized under No. **7676**, Volume **1**, dated **04/12/2005**
and represented by Mr. **Salah Abdulaziz Abdulrahman Al-Bahar <orig>صلاح عبد العزيز عبد الرحمن البحر</orig>** – of Kuwaiti nationality – holding Civil ID No. (**266040900087**) in his capacity as the Chairman of the Board of Directors of the company, pursuant to a certificate of incumbency
issued by the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> dated **05/03/2024**.

**Third Party / Founder**
Al-Tamdeen Investments Holding Company <orig>شركة التمدين للاستثمارات القابضة</orig>, of Kuwaiti nationality, Card No.
**2965420**, a Kuwaiti Closed Shareholding Company
Whose Articles of Association were notarized under No. **942**, Volume **1**, dated **02/03/2009**, and represented by
Mr. **Taq Abdulhassan Rashid Al-Hulaibi <orig>طاق عبد الحسن راشد الحليبي</orig>** – of Kuwaiti nationality –
holding Civil ID No. (**262051000318**) in his capacity as the Chairman of the Board
of Directors of the company, pursuant to a certificate of incumbency issued by the Ministry of
Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> dated **25/07/2024**.

**Fourth Party / Founder**
Al-Madina Al-Thaniya for Trading and Contracting Company <orig>شركه المدينة الثانية للتجارة والمقاولات</orig>, of Kuwaiti nationality, Card
No. **2582029**, a Limited Liability Company, whose Articles of Association were notarized
under No. **5422**, Volume **1**, and amended by several deeds, the last of which was notarized under No. **4994**,
Volume **1**, dated **20/09/2012**, and represented by Mr. **Azzam Hamza**
**Abdulaziz Al-Humaidi <orig>عزام حمزة عبد العزيز الحميدي</orig>** – of Kuwaiti nationality – holding Civil ID No.
(**265021700026**) in his capacity as an authorized signatory, pursuant to an

Card No. 2965941, a Limited Liability Company <orig>شركة ذات مسؤولية محدودة</orig>, its articles of association <orig>عقد تأسيسها</orig> notarized under No. 5187, Volume 1, dated 6/7/2008, and amended by several contracts, the last of which is the contract notarized under No. 4993, Volume 1, dated 20/9/2012.
Its signatory representative is Mr. Azzam Hamza Abdul Aziz Al-Humaidi <orig>عزام حمزة عبد العزيز الحميدي</orig> – Kuwaiti national – holding card No. (265021700026) in his capacity as an authorized signatory for the company, by virtue of an extract certificate issued by the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> dated 20/1/2025.
They, being of full legal capacity, requested the notarization of the following contract:
Company Name: Tamdeen International Hotels <orig>التمدين العالمية للفنادق</orig>
Its Type: A Kuwaiti Closed Shareholding Company <orig>شركة مساهمة كويتية مقفلة</orig>
Company Capital: 20,000,000 / Twenty Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only.

Preamble
The founders acknowledge their legal capacity to establish a Kuwaiti closed shareholding company <orig>شركة مساهمة كويتية مقفلة</orig> among themselves and their commitment to the rules stipulated for its establishment in accordance with the provisions of Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig>, its amendments, and its executive regulations.
They also acknowledge their commitment to all rules stipulated for the company's establishment in accordance with the provisions of the following articles:

Article (1)
The preceding preamble is considered an integral part of this contract.

Article (2)
The founders acknowledge that the company was established in accordance with the provisions of Companies Law No. (1) of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم (1) لسنة 2016</orig>, its amendments, its executive regulations, and the provisions of this contract.
The company shall acquire legal personality <orig>الشخصية الاعتبارية</orig> from the date of registration.
It may not commence its activities except from the date of registration and the approval of all regulatory bodies <orig>الجهات الرقابية</orig> for its engagement in the activity.

Article (3)
Company Name: Tamdeen International Hotels <orig>التمدين العالمية للفنادق</orig> / A Kuwaiti Closed Shareholding Company <orig>شركة مساهمة كويتية مقفلة</orig>.

Article (4)
The company's main headquarters <orig>المركز الرئيسي</orig> is located in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, and its domicile is in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>. The partners may transfer the main headquarters to any other location within Kuwait, and open branches and agencies for the company inside and outside the State of Kuwait. The company may carry out the aforementioned activities in the State of Kuwait and abroad, either directly or by agency. The company may also engage in similar, complementary, necessary, or related activities to its stated purposes.
The company's headquarters is considered its legal domicile <orig>الموطن القانوني</orig> for directing correspondence and judicial notices to it, and its data shall be recorded in the Commercial Register <orig>السجل التجاري</orig>. Any change to this headquarters shall not be recognized until it is registered in the Commercial Register.

Article (5)
The company's duration is unlimited, commencing from the date of registration.

Article (6)
Without prejudice to the provisions of Decree-Law No. 1/2016 <orig>المرسوم بقانون الشركات رقم 2016/1</orig> concerning companies, its amendments, and its executive regulations, the purposes for which the company was established are:

<table_caption>Company Activities and Codes</table_caption>
<table>
| Activity Code | Activity Name |
|:---|:---|
| 681010    | Buying and Selling Land and Real Estate |
| 681012    | Buying and Selling Products |
| 681020    | Management and Leasing of Owned or Leased Real Estate |
| 681022    | Management and Leasing of Owned or Leased Real Estate (Non-Residential) |
| 681091    | Ownership of Real Estate and Movable Assets for the Company's Benefit |
| 682021    | Management of Third-Party Properties |
| 682022    | Management and Development of Land and Real Estate |
| 681031    | Management and Operation of Hotels |
</table>
The company may carry out the aforementioned activities in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> and abroad, either directly or by agency. The company may also engage in similar, complementary, necessary, or related activities to its stated purposes.

Article (7)
The company's financial year <orig>السنة المالية</orig> begins on January 1st and ends on December 31st of each year. The first financial year is an exception, commencing from the date of the company's registration in the Commercial Register <orig>السجل التجاري</orig> and ending on December 31st of the following financial year.

Article (8)
The company's authorized, issued, and paid-up capital <orig>رأس مال الشركة المصرح به والمصدر والمدفوع</orig> is set at only K.D. 20,000,000 (Twenty Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), distributed over (200,000,000 shares), with each share valued at (100 fils). All shares are cash shares.

Article (9)
The founders, signatories to the contract, have subscribed to the full company capital as follows:

<table_caption>Shareholder Contributions to Company Capital</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Shareholder Name | Number of Shares | Value in Kuwaiti Dinars |
|:--|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | Tamdeen Investment Company <orig>شركة التمدين الاستثمارية</orig> | 199800000 | 19980000 |
| 2 | Wafra Holding Company <orig>شركة وفرة القابضة</orig> | 50000     | 5000     |
| 3 | Tamdeen Franchises Holding Company <orig>شركة التمدين للامتيازات القابضة</orig> | 50000     | 5000     |
| 4 | Al-Madina Al-Thaniya General Trading and Contracting Company <orig>شركة المدينة الثانية للتجارة العامة والمقاولات</orig> | 50000     | 5000     |
| 5 | Tamdeen Al-Oula Company for Buying and Selling Real Estate and Land <orig>شركة التمدين الأولى لبيع وشراء العقارات والأراضي</orig> | 50000     | 5000     |
|   | Total | 200000000 | 20000000 |
</table>
The founders acknowledge that they have deposited the value of the company's cash capital at a rate of (100%) of the company's cash capital from the total value of the shares they subscribed to, amounting to (K.D. 20,000,000), each according to their subscription ratio, with the National Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الوطني</orig>, by virtue of the certificate issued by the aforementioned bank and dated (14/01/2025), attached to the original of this contract.

Article (10)
The expenses, wages, disbursements, and costs that the company committed to pay due to its establishment amount to (K.D. 3,000) according to the statement attached to the original contract, included in the general expenses account.

## Article (11)

The founders signing this contract undertake to carry out all necessary procedures to complete the establishment of the company and commit to excluding and canceling fictitious and duplicate subscription requests and taking the necessary measures to achieve this.
For this purpose, they have appointed Mr. Azzam Hamza Abdul Aziz Al-Humaidi <orig>عزام حمزة عبد العزيز الحميدي</orig> to take legal actions, complete the necessary documents, and introduce any amendments that official authorities deem necessary to be included in the contract or in its attached Articles of Association.
Within three months from the date of completion of the subscription and before the constituent assembly meeting, the founders must submit to the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> a statement detailing the number of shares subscribed to by each founder, their remaining balances, the payment of due installments, their prices, their addresses, the share value, and the amount paid thereof.

## Article (12)

The founders of the company shall be jointly and severally liable among themselves for compensating any damage incurred by the company, its shareholders, or third parties due to the invalidity of the company's contract or its Articles of Association.

Al-Tamdeen International Hotels Company <orig>شركة التمدين العالمية للفنادق</orig>
Kuwaiti Closed Shareholding Company
(K.C.S.C.)
Company Establishment
A- Elements of Company Establishment

## Article (1)

The company was established in accordance with the provisions of Companies Law No. 1/2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 2016/1</orig> and its amendments and executive regulations, and these Articles of Association, among the shareholders whose provisions are detailed hereinafter, as a Kuwaiti Closed Shareholding Company (K.C.S.C.).

## Article (2)

The company's main headquarters and legal domicile are in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, which is the address relied upon for directing correspondence and judicial notices. Any change to this domicile shall not be recognized unless it is registered in the Commercial Register. The Board of Directors may establish branches, agencies, or offices for it within the State of Kuwait or abroad.

## Article (3)

The duration of this company is indefinite and commences from the date of registration.

## Article (4)

Without prejudice to the provisions of Companies Law No. 1/2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 2016/1</orig> and its amendments and executive regulations, the purposes for which the company was established are:

<table_caption>Company Activities and Codes</table_caption>
<table>
| Activity Code | Activity Name |
|:---|:---|
| 681010    | Buying and Selling Land and Real Estate |
| 681012    | Buying and Selling Products |
| 681020    | Management and Leasing of Owned or Leased Real Estate |
| 681022    | Management and Leasing of Owned or Leased Real Estate (Non-Residential) |
</table>

<table_caption>Company Activities and Codes</table_caption>
<table>
| Activity Code | Activity Name |
|:---|:---|
| 681091    | Ownership of Real Estate and Contracting for the Company's Benefit |
| 682021    | Management of Third-Party Properties |
| 682022    | Management and Development of Land and Real Estate |
| 681031    | Management and Operation of Hotels |
</table>

B- Capital and Methods of Increasing It

## Article (5)

The authorized, issued, and paid-up capital has been set at (K.D. 20,000,000) (Twenty Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only), fully paid in cash.
The company's issued capital consists of cash shares paid by the National Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الوطني</orig> as per the bank's certificate dated 14/01/2025 AD.

## Article (6)

The company's shares are nominal and may not be owned by non-Kuwaitis in accordance with the provisions of the law and the ministerial decisions regulating this.

## Article (7)

The authorized capital may not be increased unless the value of the original shares has been fully paid. The Extraordinary General Assembly may authorize the Board of Directors to determine the date of its implementation. However, by a resolution of the company's Board of Directors, the issued capital may be increased within the limits of the authorized capital, provided that the issued capital has been fully paid.
New shares may not be issued for less than their nominal value.

## Article (8)

If the value of the original shares has been fully paid, the company's authorized capital may be increased by a resolution issued by the Extraordinary General Assembly after the approval of the regulatory authorities, based on a reasoned proposal from the Board of Directors and a report from the auditor in this regard, provided that the resolution issued for the capital increase specifies the amount and methods of the increase.

## Article (9)

If a capital increase is decided and some shareholders do not exercise their priority right to subscribe to the capital increase shares, the unsubscribed shares shall be allocated to those shareholders of the company who wish to subscribe. If the subscription requests exceed the number of offered shares, they shall be allocated to the subscribers proportionally to their subscribed amounts.
In all cases where the entire new shares are not subscribed to, the Board of Directors may allocate the unsubscribed shares to new shareholders, and the unsubscribed new shares shall be considered canceled by operation of law.

## Article (10)

The company may increase its capital through public subscription as stipulated in Article (160) of Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig> and its amendments and executive regulations.

## Article (11)

The shareholder's right to dispose of their shares is restricted by one or both of the following restrictions:
1- Requiring a priority right for the company's shareholders to purchase shares that

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
85
</header>


### Article (19)
The founders must invite the Constituent Assembly <orig>الجمعية التأسيسية</orig> to convene within three months from the date of completion of the subscription. If the period expires without the assembly being held, the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> shall, within fifteen days from the date of expiry of the said period, invite the Constituent Assembly <orig>الجمعية التأسيسية</orig> to convene.

### Article (20)
The invitation to attend the meeting of the Constituent Assembly <orig>الجمعية التأسيسية</orig> shall include the agenda, time, and place of the meeting, and shall be sent by one of the following methods:
1.  Registered letters sent to all subscribers at least two weeks before the scheduled date of the meeting.
2.  Announcement, which must be made twice, provided that the second announcement is made after a period of no less than seven days from the date of publication of the first announcement and at least seven days before the meeting.
3.  Hand delivery of the invitation to shareholders or their legal representatives at least one day before the meeting, with an endorsement on a copy of the invitation confirming receipt.
4.  Any other modern means of communication specified in the Executive Regulations of the Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig>. The Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> must be notified in writing of the agenda, date, and place of the meeting at least seven days before its convening for its representative to attend. The person elected by the Assembly for this purpose shall preside over the meeting of the Constituent Assembly <orig>الجمعية التأسيسية</orig>.

### Article (21)
The meeting of the Constituent Assembly <orig>الجمعية التأسيسية</orig> shall not be valid unless attended by shareholders with voting rights representing more than half of the subscribed shares. If this quorum is not met, the Assembly must be invited to a second meeting with the same agenda, to be held within a period of no less than seven days and no more than thirty days from the date of the first meeting. The second meeting shall be valid regardless of the number of attendees.
A new invitation for the second meeting may not be required if its date was specified in the invitation to the first meeting. Decisions shall be issued by an absolute majority of the shares present at the meeting.

### Article (22)
The founders shall submit to the Constituent Assembly <orig>الجمعية التأسيسية</orig> a report containing comprehensive information about all incorporation operations and the amounts spent, along with supporting documents. This report shall be placed in a location specified by the founders for subscribers to review.

Its owner wishes to sell them.
2- Requiring the Board of Directors' <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> approval for the buyer of the shares.
Dispositions referred to in Article (172) of the Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig> are excluded from these two restrictions.
(This provision does not apply to companies listed on the stock exchange.)

### Article (12)
(Mandatory text if the first restriction of Article 11 of these Articles of Association <orig>النظام</orig> is adopted) The shareholder must notify the company of the terms of sale before disposing of their shares. The disposition of shares shall not be effective until ten days have passed from the date of notification without any of the shareholders submitting a request to purchase the shares. If a shareholder submits a request to purchase the shares, this must be done at the price stated in the terms of sale.

### Article (13)
(Mandatory text if the second restriction of Article 11 of these Articles of Association <orig>النظام</orig> is adopted) Without prejudice to the provisions regarding the company's purchase of its own shares, the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>, in case of rejecting the buyer's person, must purchase the shares on behalf of the company within ten days from the date the Board <orig>المجلس</orig> is notified of the request for approval. The purchase in this case shall be at the price at which the shareholder agreed to sell their shares.

## Subscription
### Article (14)
The founders who signed the Articles of Incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> subscribed to the entire capital of the company with shares totaling 200,000,000 shares (two hundred million shares) with a nominal value of 20,000,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (twenty million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only), distributed among them, each according to their subscription ratio specified in the Articles of Incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig>. An amount of 20,000,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (twenty million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only) of the nominal value of the shares they subscribed to has been paid to (National Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الوطني</orig>) as per the attached bank certificate dated 14/01/2025 AD.

### Article (15)
Ownership of a share inevitably entails the shareholder's acceptance of the provisions of the Articles of Incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig>, the provisions of the Company's Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي للشركة</orig>, and the resolutions of its General Assemblies <orig>جمعياتها العامة</orig>.

### Article (16)
Each share entitles its owner to an equal share, without discrimination, in the ownership of the company's assets and in the distributed profits.

### Article (17)
The company shall have a special register kept with a clearing agency <orig>وكالة مقاصة</orig>, in which the names of shareholders, their nationalities, domiciles, the number and type of shares owned by each of them, and the value paid for each share shall be recorded.
Any changes occurring to the data recorded therein shall be endorsed in the shareholders' register in accordance with what the company or the clearing agency <orig>وكالة المقاصة</orig> receives, and it shall be provided with the data of this register.
<page_end>85</page_end>

thereon, at least seven days before the General Assembly meeting, and this shall be indicated in the invitation to subscribers to attend the meeting.

## Article (23)
The Constituent Assembly <orig>الجمعية التأسيسية</orig> shall be competent to address the following matters:
1. Approving the company's incorporation procedures after verifying their validity and compliance with the provisions of the Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig> and the company's Articles of Association <orig>عقد الشركة</orig>.
2. Approving the valuation of in-kind shares, if any, as stipulated in Article (11) of the Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig>.
3. Electing the members of the first Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>.
4. Selecting the auditor <orig>مراقب الحسابات</orig> and determining their fees.
5. Finally declaring the company's incorporation.
A copy of the minutes of the Constituent Assembly <orig>الجمعية التأسيسية</orig> meeting, including the resolutions adopted, shall be sent to the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
The first Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall publish the company's Articles of Association <orig>عقد الشركة</orig> and register it in the Commercial Register <orig>السجل التجاري</orig> within thirty days from the date of the final declaration of the company's incorporation.
Rights and Obligations of Shareholders

## Article (24)
A member of the company shall specifically enjoy the following rights:
1. Receiving profits and obtaining bonus shares <orig>أسهم المنحة</orig> that are decided for distribution.
2. Participating in the company's management through membership in the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> and attending General Assemblies <orig>الجمعيات العامة</orig> and participating in their deliberations, in accordance with the provisions of the Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig> and these Articles of Association <orig>النظام</orig>. Any agreement to the contrary shall be null and void.
3. Obtaining, at least seven days before the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> meeting, the company's financial statements <orig>البيانات المالية</orig> for the expired accounting period, the Board of Directors' <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> report, and the auditor's <orig>مراقب الحسابات</orig> report.
4. Disposing of the shares owned by them and having priority in subscribing to new shares.
5. Receiving a share of the company's assets upon liquidation after settling its debts.

## Article (25)
A member of the company shall specifically be obligated to:
1. Pay the installments due on the shares they own upon their due dates and pay compensation for delay in payment.
2. Pay the expenses incurred by the company for unpaid installments of their share value. The company may execute on the shares to recover its rights.
3. Implement the resolutions issued by the company's General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>.
4. Refrain from any act that harms the financial or moral interests of the company and be obligated to compensate for damages arising from violating this.

## Article (26)
The General Assembly of Shareholders <orig>الجمعية العامة للمساهمين</orig> may not:
1. Increase the financial burdens of the shareholder or increase the nominal value of the shares.
2. Decrease the percentage of net profits to be distributed to shareholders as specified in the company's Articles of Association <orig>عقد الشركة</orig>.
3. Impose new conditions not mentioned in the Articles of Incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> or these Articles of Association <orig>النظام</orig> related to the shareholder's right to attend and vote in General Assemblies <orig>الجمعيات العامة</orig>.
These provisions may be deviated from with the written acceptance of all shareholders or by a collective vote involving all shareholders, and by completing the necessary procedures to amend the company's Articles of Association <orig>عقد الشركة</orig>.
A- Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>

## Article (27)
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> consisting of three members. The term of membership shall be three years, renewable.
If it is not possible to elect a new Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> within the specified period, the existing Board shall continue to manage the company's affairs until the reasons cease to exist and a new Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> is elected.

## Article (28)
Shareholders shall elect the members of the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> by secret ballot. The company's Articles of Association <orig>عقد الشركة</orig> may stipulate that no more than half of the members of the first Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall be elected from among the company's founders.

## Article (29)
The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall elect by secret ballot a Chairman <orig>رئيساً للمجلس</orig> and a Vice-Chairman <orig>نائباً للرئيس</orig>. The Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall represent the company in its relations with third parties and before the judiciary, in addition to other competencies specified in the Articles of Association <orig>العقد</orig>. His signature shall be considered as the signature of the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> in the company's relations with third parties. He shall implement the Board's resolutions and adhere to its recommendations. The Vice-Chairman <orig>نائب الرئيس</orig> shall act in place of the Chairman <orig>الرئيس</orig> in his absence or if he is prevented from exercising his powers.

## Article (30)
The company may have a Chief Executive Officer <orig>رئيساً تنفيذياً</orig> appointed by the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> from among its members or from outside, entrusted with the management of the company. The Board shall determine his allocations and powers to sign on behalf of the company.

## Article (31)
The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> may distribute work among its members according to the nature of the company's business. The Board may also delegate one of its members, a committee of its members, or a third party to perform one or more specific tasks, supervise an aspect of the company's activity, or exercise some of the powers or competencies entrusted to the Board.

## Article (32)
Any shareholder, whether a natural or legal person, may appoint representatives to the company's Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> in proportion to the shares they own in it. The number of Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> members selected in this manner shall be deducted from the total number of Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> members to be elected. Shareholders who have representatives on the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> may not participate with other shareholders in electing the remaining members of the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> except to the extent exceeding the proportion used in appointing their representatives to the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>. A group of shareholders may form an alliance among themselves to appoint one or more representatives for them on the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> in proportion to their combined ownership.
<page_end>86</page_end>

<page_start>87</page_start>
<page_metadata>

  "page_title": "Kuwait Today Official Gazette - Company Law Articles on Board of Directors <orig>الكويت اليوم - مواد قانون الشركات بشأن مجلس الإدارة</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-02-02",
  "issue_number": 1724,

  "page_summary": "This page from the Kuwait Today Official Gazette presents several articles (33-42) of company law, detailing regulations for the Board of Directors, including election procedures, meeting protocols, member eligibility, restrictions on activities, confidentiality, and compensation."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
87
</header>

These representatives shall have the same rights and duties as elected members. The shareholder shall be a representative responsible for the company's actions, its creditors, and its shareholders.

### Article (33)
A Board of Directors meeting shall not be valid unless attended by at least half of the members, excluding those not counted from three. A larger percentage or number may be agreed upon. Meetings may be held using modern communication methods, and decisions may be passed by circulation with the approval of all Board members.
The Board of Directors must meet at least six times during the year, and a greater number of meetings may be agreed upon.

### Article (34)
Minutes of the Board of Directors meetings shall be recorded and signed by the attending members, the Board Secretary, and any member who did not approve a decision taken by the Board may record their objection in the meeting minutes.

### Article (35)
If a Board of Directors member's position becomes vacant, it shall be filled by the shareholder who received the most votes among those who did not win Board membership. If there is an impediment to the next in line, the new member shall complete only the term of their predecessor.
However, if the vacant positions reach one-quarter of the original positions, the Board of Directors must call a General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> of shareholders to convene within two months from the date the last position became vacant, and elect those who will fill the vacant positions.

### Article (36)
The following conditions must be met by anyone nominated for Board of Directors membership:
1.  Must possess legal capacity to act.
2.  Must not have been previously convicted of a felony with a custodial sentence, or a crime of bankruptcy due to negligence or fraud, or a crime against honor or trust, or a custodial sentence for violating legal provisions, unless their rehabilitation has been restored.
3.  Must personally own, or the person they represent must own, a number of the company's shares.
If a Board of Directors member loses any of the aforementioned conditions, their membership shall cease.

### Article (37)
Membership in the company's Board of Directors shall not be included in the maximum number of
memberships referred to in Article (234) of the Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig>.
A person may be the chairman of the Board of Directors of more than one closed joint-stock company.

### Article (38)
The chairman or a member of the Board of Directors, even if representing a natural or legal person, may not exploit information obtained by virtue of their position to gain benefit for themselves or others.
A Board of Directors member may dispose of their shares in the company during their membership on the Board, without prejudice to the restrictions on share disposal stipulated in the Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig>, the company's articles of association, or these regulations.

### Article (39)
Board of Directors members may not disclose to shareholders, outside of General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> meetings, or to third parties, any company secrets they became aware of due to their management duties. Otherwise, they shall be dismissed and held accountable for compensating damages resulting from the violation.

### Article (40)
The chairman of the Board of Directors or any of its members may not combine membership in the Board of Directors of two competing companies, or participate in any work that would compete with the company, or trade for their own account or for the account of others in any branch of activity carried out by the company. Otherwise, the company shall have the right to demand compensation from them or to consider the operations they carried out for their own account as if they were conducted for the company's account, unless this is done with the approval of the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig>.

### Article (41)
The total remuneration of the chairman and members of the Board of Directors may not exceed ten percent of the net profit after deducting depreciation and reserves and distributing a profit of not less than 5% of the capital to shareholders (a higher percentage may be agreed upon).
An annual remuneration not exceeding six thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> may be distributed to the chairman of the Board of Directors and to each member of this Board from the date of the company's establishment until profits are achieved that allow for the distribution of remuneration in accordance with the preceding paragraph. By a resolution issued by the company's General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>, an independent Board member may be exempted from the aforementioned maximum remuneration (if the company has independent members).
The Board of Directors is obligated to submit an annual report to be presented to the company's Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> for approval, provided that it accurately includes a detailed statement of the amounts, benefits, and advantages received by the Board of Directors, regardless of their nature or designation.

### Article (42)
It is not permissible for anyone who has a representative on the Board of Directors, or for the chairman or a member of the Board of Directors, or a member of the executive management, or their spouses, or
<page_end>87</page_end>

<page_start>88</page_start>
<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Kuwait Today - Issue 1724, Volume 71: Corporate Governance and General Assembly Regulations <orig>الكويت اليوم العدد 1724 السنة الحادية والسبعون: أحكام حوكمة الشركات والجمعية العامة</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-02-02",
  "issue_number": 1724,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": ["ar"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": null,
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page outlines articles from Kuwaiti corporate law, detailing regulations concerning conflicts of interest for board members, their responsibilities, shareholder rights in general assembly meetings, and the powers and procedures of the ordinary general assembly, including financial reporting and election processes."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724 Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
88
</header>

### Article (43)
The company may not lend to any of its board members, or the Chief Executive Officer, or their spouses, or their relatives up to the second degree, or their affiliated companies, unless there is an authorization from the company's Ordinary General Assembly. Any action taken in violation thereof shall not be enforceable against the company, without prejudice to the rights of bona fide third parties (this provision does not apply to companies authorized to lend).

### Article (44)
The Chairman of the Board of Directors and its members are responsible towards the company, shareholders, and third parties for all acts of fraud, abuse of authority, any violation of the law or the company's articles of association, or for errors in management. A vote by the General Assembly to discharge the Board of Directors shall not prevent the filing of a liability lawsuit. Board members may not participate in voting on General Assembly resolutions related to their discharge from liability for their management, or those concerning a special benefit for them, their spouses, or their first-degree relatives, or an existing dispute between them and the company.

### Article (45)
The liability stipulated in the preceding article shall be either personal liability attaching to a specific member, or joint liability among all members of the Board of Directors. In the latter case, all members shall be jointly and severally liable to pay compensation, except for those who objected to the decision that established the liability and recorded their objection in the minutes.

### Article (46)
The company may file a liability lawsuit against the members of the Board of Directors due to errors that cause damage to the company. If the company is in liquidation, the liquidator shall undertake to file the lawsuit.

### Article (47)
Any shareholder may individually file a liability lawsuit on behalf of the company if the company fails to do so. In this case, the company must be joined as a party to be awarded compensation if warranted. A shareholder may file a personal lawsuit for compensation if the error has caused them damage, and any agreement to the contrary shall be null and void.

### Article (48)
B – General Assembly
The annual Ordinary General Assembly shall convene upon an invitation from the Board of Directors within three months following the end of the financial year, at the time and place designated by the Board of Directors. The Board may invite the General Assembly to meet whenever necessary. The Board of Directors must issue an invitation for the General Assembly to meet based on a reasoned request from a number of shareholders owning ten percent of the company's capital, or upon the request of the auditor, within fifteen days from the date of the request. The agenda shall be prepared by the inviting party. The provisions related to the Constituent Assembly stipulated in Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig> and its amendments shall apply to the procedures for inviting the General Assembly, the quorum for attendance, and voting.

### Article (49)
Every shareholder, regardless of the number of their shares, has the right to attend the General Assembly and shall have a number of votes equal to the number of votes allocated to the same class of shares. A shareholder may not vote on their own behalf or on behalf of someone they represent in matters related to a special benefit for them, or an existing dispute between them and the company. Any condition or resolution that violates this shall be null and void. A shareholder may delegate another person to attend on their behalf by virtue of a special power of attorney or an authorization prepared by the company for this purpose. Anyone claiming a right over shares that conflicts with what is recorded in the company's shareholders' register may apply to the judge of urgent matters to issue an order on petition to deprive the disputed shares of voting for a period specified by the judge or until the dispute is settled by the competent court, in accordance with the procedures stipulated in the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات المدنية والتجارية</orig>.

### Article (50)
The General Assembly meeting shall be chaired by the Chairman of the Board of Directors, or his deputy, or someone delegated by the Board of Directors for that purpose, or someone elected by the General Assembly from among the shareholders or others.

### Article (51)
Subject to the provisions of the law, the Ordinary General Assembly, in its annual meeting, shall be competent to make decisions on matters falling within its jurisdiction, and in particular the following:
1. The Board of Directors' report on the company's activity and financial position for the ended financial year.
2. The auditor's report on the company's financial statements.
3. A report on any violations detected by regulatory authorities and for which penalties were imposed on the company.
4. The company's financial statements.
5. The Board of Directors' proposals regarding profit distribution.
6. Discharge of the Board of Directors' members.
7. Election or dismissal of Board of Directors' members and determination of their remuneration.
8. Appointment of the company's auditor, and determination of their fees or delegation of the Board of Directors in this regard.
9. Report on transactions that have occurred or will occur with related parties,
<page_end>88</page_end>

<page_start>89</page_start>
<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Corporate Regulations from Al-Kuwait Al-Youm Official Gazette <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-02-02",
  "issue_number": 1724,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": ["ar"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": null,
  "publisher": "Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page details regulations concerning general assembly meetings, decision-making processes, financial year, and mandatory reserve allocations for companies, as published in the official gazette."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724 Seventy-First Year
89
</header>

### Article (52)
By a resolution issued by the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> of the company, the chairman or one or more members of the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> may be dismissed, or the company's Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> may be dissolved and a new Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> elected. This shall be based on a proposal submitted by a number of shareholders owning no less than one-quarter of the company's issued capital. If a resolution is issued to dissolve the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> and it is not possible to elect a new board at the same meeting, the Assembly <orig>الجمعية</orig> may decide either that the existing board continues to manage the company's affairs until a new board is elected, or to appoint a temporary administrative committee whose primary task is to call the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> to elect the new board, within one month of its appointment.
### Article (53)
The Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> may not discuss matters not included in the agenda unless they are urgent matters that arose after the agenda was prepared or became apparent during the meeting, or if requested by one of the supervisory authorities <orig>الجهات الرقابية</orig>, the auditor <orig>مراقب الحسابات</orig>, or a number of shareholders owning five percent of the company's capital. If, during the discussion, it becomes apparent that the information related to some of the presented matters is insufficient, the meeting must be postponed for a period not exceeding ten days if requested by a number of shareholders owning one-quarter of the issued capital. The postponed meeting shall be convened without the need for new invitation procedures.
### Article (54)
The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> must implement the resolutions of the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> unless those resolutions violate the law, the articles of incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig>, or these bylaws. The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> must re-present the violating resolutions to the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> in a meeting called to discuss the aspects of the violation.
### Article (55)
The provisions related to the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العادية</orig> shall apply to the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig>, taking into account the provisions stipulated in the following articles:
### Article (56)
The Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> shall convene upon an invitation from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> or upon a reasoned request from shareholders representing fifteen percent of the company's issued capital or from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>. The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> must invite the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> to a meeting within thirty days from the date of submitting the request. If the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> fails to invite the Assembly <orig>الجمعية</orig> within the period stipulated in the preceding paragraph, the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> shall issue the invitation for the meeting within fifteen days from the date of expiry of the period referred to in the preceding paragraph.
### Article (57)
The meeting of the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> shall not be valid unless attended by shareholders representing three-quarters of the company's issued capital. If this quorum is not met, an invitation shall be issued for a second meeting, which shall be valid if attended by those representing more than half of the issued capital. Resolutions shall be issued by a majority exceeding half of the total shares of the company's issued capital.
### Article (58)
Subject to other competencies stipulated by law, the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> shall be competent in the following matters:
1. Amending the company's articles of association <orig>عقد الشركة</orig>.
2. Selling the entire project for which the company was established or disposing of it in any other way.
3. Dissolving the company, or its merger, transformation, or division.
4. Increasing or decreasing the company's capital.
### Article (59)
Any resolution issued by the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> shall not be effective until the publication procedures <orig>إجراءات الشهر</orig> are taken. The approval of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> must be obtained if the resolution relates to the company's name, objectives, or capital.
### Article (60)
Any shareholder may file a lawsuit for the nullity of any resolution issued by the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> or the Ordinary or Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية أو غير العادية</orig> that violates the law, the company's articles of incorporation <orig>عقد تأسيس الشركة</orig>, or these bylaws, or if it is intended to harm the company's interests, and claim compensation when necessary. Resolutions of the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> that prejudice the rights of the minority may also be challenged. The challenge shall be made by a number of the company's shareholders owning fifteen percent of the company's issued capital, provided they were not among those who approved those resolutions.
## Company Accounts
### Article (61)
The company's financial year <orig>السنة المالية</orig> begins on January 1st and ends on December 31st of each year. The first financial year <orig>السنة المالية الأولى</orig> of the company is an exception, as it begins from the date of the company's registration in the commercial register <orig>السجل التجاري</orig> and ends on December 31st of the following financial year.
### Article (62)
Annually, by a resolution issued by the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>, a percentage of no less than ten percent of the net profits shall be deducted to form a statutory reserve <orig>احتياطي إجباري</orig> for the company. The Assembly <orig>الجمعية</orig> may cease this deduction if the statutory reserve <orig>الاحتياطي الإجباري</orig> exceeds half of the company's issued capital. The statutory reserve <orig>الاحتياطي الإجباري</orig> may only be used to cover the company's losses or to ensure the distribution of dividends to shareholders at a rate not exceeding five percent of the paid-up capital <orig>رأس المال المدفوع</orig> in years when the company's profits do not allow for the distribution of this percentage, due to the absence of an optional reserve <orig>احتياطي اختياري</orig> that would permit the distribution of this percentage of profits.

The provisions of Companies Law No. 1/2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 2016/1</orig> and its amendments and executive regulations shall apply to all matters not specifically provided for in the Articles of Association or in these Bylaws.

### Article (72)
An original copy of this contract shall be kept at the company's main office and on its website. An original copy of this contract shall also be kept in the company's file with the competent department at the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.

### Article (73)
The founders acknowledge the following:
First: That they have subscribed to all shares and deposited the amount required by law to be paid from their value in one of the local banks at the company's disposal.
Second: That they have appointed the necessary administrative bodies for the company's management.
Third: The preservation of supporting papers and documents for the aforementioned declarations along with the official minutes.

### Article (74)
This contract was drawn up based on the letter from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> No. 2012202438757, and registered with the Contracts and Companies Control Department <orig>مراقبة العقود والشركات</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig> under automated number 6345695 on 23/1/2025.

| 9 | Abdul Rashid Fadl <orig>عبد الرشيد فضل</orig> | 2025/57 |
| 10 | Fahad Khalid Fahad Al-Azmi <orig>فهد خالد فهد العازمي</orig> | 2025/58 |
| 11 | Reem Nasser Ahmed Boura'a <orig>ريم ناصر أحمد بوريراع</orig> | 2025/59 |
| 12 | Ali Hassan Ali Al-Sayigh <orig>علي حسن علي الصايغ</orig> | 2025/60 |
| 13 | Awatef Barrak Saif Al-Azmi <orig>عواطف براك سيف العازمي</orig> | 2025/61 |
| 14 | Saad Abdullah Abdul Hassan Al-Sharhan <orig>سعد عبد الله عبد الحسن الشرهان</orig> | 2025/62 |
| 15 | Ahmed Mohamed Qutb Metwally <orig>أحمد محمد قطب متولي</orig> | 2025/63 |
| 16 | Hammadi Abdul Malik Ahmed Mohamed <orig>حمادي عبد المالك أحمد محمد</orig> | 2025/64 |
</table>

Any amount deducted from the statutory reserve must be returned to it when the profits of subsequent years allow, unless this reserve exceeds half of the issued capital.
Additionally, one percent (1%) shall be deducted and allocated to the account of the Kuwait Foundation for the Advancement of Sciences <orig>مؤسسة الكويت للتقدم العلمي</orig> from the company's net profit.

### Article (63)
Annually, a percentage shall be deducted from the gross profits, to be determined by the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> after consulting the auditor, for the depreciation of the company's assets or to compensate for their decrease in value. These funds shall be used to purchase necessary materials, machinery, and facilities or to repair them, and these funds may not be distributed to shareholders.

### Article (64)
The General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> must decide to deduct a percentage of profits to meet the company's obligations under labor laws and social insurance laws.
A special fund may be established to assist the company's workers and employees.

### Article (65)
Annually, by a resolution issued by the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>, a percentage not exceeding ten percent of the net profits may be deducted to form an optional reserve allocated for purposes determined by the Assembly.

### Article (66)
The General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>, based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>, may distribute profits to shareholders at the end of the fiscal year. For this distribution to be valid, it must be from actual profits, in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles, and must not affect the company's paid-up capital.
Auditor

### Article (67)
The provisions of Articles 227 to 233 of Companies Law No. 1/2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 2016/01</orig> and its amendments shall apply.

### Article (68)
At the end of each fiscal year, the company must prepare a consolidated balance sheet and statements of profit and loss for itself and all its affiliated partners, accompanied by explanations and data as required by international accounting standards.
## Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company

### Article (69)
The company shall be dissolved by one of the matters stipulated in Articles 266 to 277 of the Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig> and its amendments and executive regulations.

### Article (70)
The liquidation of the company shall be carried out as set forth in the provisions of Articles 278 to 295 of the Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig> and its amendments and executive regulations.
<page_end>90</page_end>

** According to the description certificate:
- No violations.
** According to the expert's report:
During the expert session dated 1/7/2023, we proceeded to the disputed property located in Al-Ardiya <orig>العارضية</orig> area, Block 3, Street 9, House 21, Plot 66, Automated Number 12803986, in the presence and under the guidance of the plaintiff personally and her agent, and the first defendant personally and in his capacity as agent for the defendants from the second to the fifth, and in the presence of the study expert engaged by the administration, Mr. Tariq Al-Moajel <orig>طارق المعجل</orig>, to assess the value of the property and the value of the usufruct for the property from 9/7/2011. The inspection revealed the following:
1. The property subject of the lawsuit is located on a single street with a back alley, bordered by a neighbor on two sides, and has a small setback at the front facade, paved and partially shaded, used for car parking.
2. The property subject of the lawsuit is a government house, old finish, with an exterior limestone cladding, and an area of (600) square meters according to the inheritance ownership document dated 6/11/2022, bearing number 11069, owned jointly by the plaintiff and the defendants from the first to the fifth, as stated in the aforementioned document.
3. The property subject of the lawsuit consists of a main building, two front annexes, and a back annex, according to the following details:
- The main building consists of a ground floor and a first floor, according to the following details:
    * The ground floor consists of a living room, a reception hall, a bathroom, a kitchen, and a maid's room with its bathroom.
    * The first floor consists of four rooms, a hall, and two bathrooms.
- The first front annex consists of a room and a bathroom, and the other annex is a storage room.
- The back annex consists of two floors, ground and first, according to the following details:
    The ground floor consists of a hall, a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig>, a room, three bathrooms, a maid's room, and a kitchen.
    The first floor consists of a room from the main structure.
The disputed property has an old finish level, with paints and flooring specified only in the main building according to the following details: the floors are ceramic, the air conditioning consists of units, the lighting is spot lights, the decorations are gypsum, and the walls have ordinary paint.
The expert examination revealed that the back annex is separate from the main building, with a separate entrance from the back alley, which the plaintiff enabled us to access as she possesses the keys to the annex, and it is completely abandoned.
The first defendant stated that the fifth defendant resides in the property and utilizes the main building and its front annexes.
The expert examination revealed that the disputed property is not leased and generates no income.
The study expert engaged by the administration inspected the property and recorded
