# Announcement of the Sale of a Share in a Property by Public Auction

The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction sale of a share in the property described below, on Monday, 3/3/2025 – Hall 48 – on the second floor of the Palace of Justice at 9:00 AM – in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2024/84 Sales /1.

### Filed by: Sanitan Ghazi Eqab Al-Mutairi <orig>صنيتان غازي عقاب المطيري</orig>

### Against:
1.  Mohammed Ali Hamad Al-Shammari <orig>محمد علي حمد الشمري</orig>.
2.  Hammad Ali Hamad Al-Shammari <orig>حماد علي حمد الشمري</orig>.
3.  Adel Miz'al Fahad Al-Shammari <orig>عادل مزعل فهد الشمري</orig>.
4.  Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>.

### Property Description: (According to the attached description certificate)
An undivided share <orig>حصة مشاعاً</orig> of 50% in the property under document No. 1992/5739, located in Al-Andalus <orig>الأندلس</orig> area – Plot No. 17 – Block No. 5 – Plan M/33782, out of its total area of 910m², to be sold by public auction for a base price of K.D. 340,000 (Three Hundred Forty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) for the offered share.

** According to the description certificate:
- Adhesion to the neighbor on the ground, first, and second floors facing the service road.
- Adhesion in the middle of the plot.
- Light material construction on the roof.

** According to the expert's report:
On 16/4/2024, the property in dispute, located in Al-Andalus <orig>الأندلس</orig> area – Block (5) – Street (1) – Plot (17) House (28), was visited in the presence and guidance of the plaintiff personally. The other parties to the lawsuit or their representatives failed to attend. In the presence of Mr. Falah Nasser Murshid <orig>فلاح ناصر مرشد</orig>, the expert of the Administration, the inspection was carried out as follows:
The property subject of the lawsuit conforms in terms of general specifications to the sale contract issued by the Real Estate Registration Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري</orig>, registered under No. (1992/5739) and with an area of 910 m², submitted by the plaintiff's agent in his document portfolio on 1/4/2024, document (1).
The property subject of the lawsuit is a private residential plot located on two streets (Street (1) and Street (102)), bordered by a neighbor on two sides, and has (4) entrances, (3) and (1) entrance facing Street (102).
The door and bell were knocked, but no one answered. Therefore, the expert of the Administration inspected the property subject of the lawsuit from the outside.
The property subject of the lawsuit consists of two parts, detailed as follows:
. The first part, with automated number (12770205), consists of a floor
Its specific observations and review of the inheritance ownership document for the property in dispute, in preparation for estimating the property's value and assessing the usufruct consideration for the property.

### - Secondly: Auction Terms:
1.  Firstly: The auction shall start at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
2.  Secondly: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
3.  Thirdly: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was initially awarded.
4.  Fourthly: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full price. In this case, the bidding will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
5.  Fifthly: If the initial bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to bid with a ten percent increase, the bidding will be immediately reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no offer not accompanied by the deposit of its full value will be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
6.  Sixthly: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transfer and registration of ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to K.D. 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
7.  Seventhly: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
8.  Eighthly: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.

### Notice:
1.  This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2.  The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3.  The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership has been divested is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."

<footer>
Chief Justice of the General Court <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

# Announcement of Property Sale by Public Auction

The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale of the property described below by public auction on Monday, 3/3/2025, in Hall 48 on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig> at 9:00 AM, in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit 2024/253 Sales/1.
Filed by: Jawahir Mohammed Jaza' Al-Ajmi <orig>جواهر محمد جازع العجمي</orig>.
Against:
1- Mohammed Jaza' Abdullah Al-Ajmi <orig>محمد جازع عبدالله العجمي</orig>.
2- Raf'ah Mohammed Jaza' Al-Ajmi <orig>رفعه محمد جازع العجمي</orig>.
3- Hammad Mohammed Jaza' Al-Ajmi <orig>حماد محمد جازع العجمي</orig>.
Property Description (according to the attached description certificate)
Property document number 1993/8946 located in Sabah Al-Salem <orig>صباح السالم</orig> area – Plot No. 120 – Block 13, Northern Part – with an area of 300.125 m2, by public auction at a price of 36873, with a basic amount of 380,000 K.D. (Three Hundred Eighty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the description certificate for the following violations:
- Full attachment from all sides on the ground floor, full attachment from the rear facade (courtyard), attachment with stones on the first floor, attachment on the surrounding side, and the presence of additional construction on the ground and first floors without a license.
** According to the expert's report:
On 17/3/2021, the site of the dispute, located in Sabah Al-Salem <orig>صباح السالم</orig> area – Block 13 – Street 1, Plot 41, was visited and inspected on-site in the presence and guidance of the appellant personally, the first respondent personally, and the agent of the second and third respondents, with the assistance of Mr. Tariq Abdullah Al-Moajel <orig>طارق عبد الله المعجل</orig>, Expert of Knowledge <orig>خبير الدراية</orig> at the department, during the inspection, as follows:
1- The property subject to the dispute is a private residence with a front, back, and a side opening onto an electrical transformer. It is bordered by neighbors on one side and has a side and rear setback. It is a government-built house with an area of 300.125 m2, renovated old construction, and fully clad with white stone on the exterior.
2- The property consists of a ground floor and a first floor, with nothing on the roof, with the following details:
a- The ground floor consists of 4 rooms + 4 bathrooms + a hall + a kitchen + a storage room.
b- The first floor consists of 5 rooms + 3 bathrooms + a large hall +

## Second: Auction Terms:

First: The auction shall start at the basic price, and participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: Whoever's bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price, otherwise the bidding shall be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was concluded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session who accepts to purchase with an increased bid, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be reopened in the same session based on this price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward to increase the bid by one-tenth, the bidding shall be immediately reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. No bid in this session shall be considered unless accompanied by a full deposit of its value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transfer and registration of ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request of those directly involved in the sale procedures, and at their responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.

</header>
# Announcement of Real Estate Sale by Public Auction

The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale of the property described below by public auction on Monday, 3/3/2025 – Hall – 48 – on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig> at 9:00 AM – in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2023/402 Sales/1 <orig>بيوع/1</orig> filed by: Adel Rashid Ali Al-Enezi <orig>عادل رشيد على العنزي</orig>.

Against:
1- Alia Jad'an Ali Al-Enezi <orig>عليا جدعان على العنزي</orig>.
2- The Director General <orig>مدير عام</orig> of the Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig> in his capacity.

Property Description: (According to the attached description certificate)
Property document No. 2017/4376 located in Abu Futaira <orig>أبو فطيرة</orig> area – Plot 393 <orig>قسيمة 393</orig> – Block No. 8 <orig>قطعة رقم 8</orig> – Plan 37883/ with an area of 400 m2, by public auction for a base price of K.D. 600,000 (Six Hundred Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).

** According to the description certificate:
- The property is located within a private residential area, consisting of a basement + ground floor + first floor + part of the second floor, and the property conforms to the plan.

** According to the expert's report:
On 14/12/2022, we moved to the disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> located in Abu Futaira <orig>أبو فطيرة</orig> area, in the presence of the plaintiff personally and his agent, the first defendant personally, and the study expert <orig>خبير الدراسة</orig>. The second defendant failed to attend. The inspection was carried out as follows:
- The disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> is located in Abu Futaira <orig>أبو فطيرة</orig> area, Block (8), Street (192), Plot (393), House No. (10), Automated Number (94085542).
- The area of the disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> is (400 m2) and it has a southern facade, conforming to ownership document No. (2010/11716).
- The disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> is bordered by a neighbor from the west and north, an alley from the east, and Street No. (192) from the south. The facade width of the disputed property is (16) meters, with a setback of (4.40 m), and the exterior cladding of the house is brown Sigma.
- The disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> has (3) entrances with the following details:
  * Main entrance on the ground floor.
  * Side entrance leading to the basement.
  * Another side entrance leading to the kitchen and serving the two apartments on the second floor.
- The disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> consists of a basement, (3) floors, and a roof with the following details:
- The basement consists of a sunken courtyard <orig>حوش ساقط</orig>, a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> with a bathroom, (1) hall, (1) room, (1) bathroom, and (2) storage rooms. There is also a driver's room with an isolated bathroom, accessible via the side entrance.
- The ground floor consists of (1) hall and (1) master bedroom with a large kitchen.
3- The exterior cladding is white stone.
4- The house air conditioning consists of split units.
5- Ceramic floors, and it does not have an elevator.
- The study expert <orig>خبير الدراسة</orig> took all specific and general observations regarding the disputed property in preparation for estimating the base price for its sale by public auction.

## Second: Auction Terms:

1.  **First:** The auction starts at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of the price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
2.  **Second:** The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
3.  **Third:** If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price, otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at his expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
4.  **Fourth:** If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to him, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
5.  **Fifth:** If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding will be immediately reopened at his expense based on the price at which it was awarded to him in the previous session. No offer in this session will be considered unless accompanied by the deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
6.  **Sixth:** In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the fees for transfer and registration of ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to K.D. 200, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
7.  **Seventh:** This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures request it at their responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
8.  **Eighth:** The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance <orig>معاينة نافية للجهالة</orig>.

Notice:
1.  This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2.  The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3.  The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership has been expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obliged to draw up a lease contract in his favor for a fair rent <orig>أجرة المثل</orig>."

## Special Conditions for Bidders

- The bidder must be Kuwaiti – an individual or a company – registered in the Commercial Register and with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>. Foreigners may participate provided they have a Kuwaiti partner or commercial agent with a notarized contract. (The following must be attached: a copy of the Chamber of Commerce and Industry certificate, a copy of the company license, a copy of the civil ID, and an authorization letter approved by the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, all of which must be valid).
- Kuwaiti individuals are permitted to participate in the auction (a copy of the civil ID must be attached).

## Special Conditions for Auction (2442)

- The successful bidder of the scrap car auction shall, at their own expense, completely remove the original color of the vehicles at their location, prior to their removal or transfer of ownership, and under the supervision of specialists from the Ministry's Machinery Department.
- The Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> is not responsible for transferring vehicle ownership to the successful bidder at the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>.

# Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig>
## Announcement
### Tender No. (DA/119/2024-2025)

The Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> announces the offering of Tender No. (DA/119/2024-
2025) for the license to exploit, manage, and operate an investment site at Sheikh Abdullah Al-Salem Cultural Centre <orig>مركز الشيخ عبدالله السالم الثقافي</orig> (a specialized local café (B+C5A)). Interested companies or institutions specialized in this field should apply to obtain the terms and conditions booklet and tender documents during official working hours from (Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> - Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> - Administrative Building - First Floor - Zone 7 - Tenders and Follow-up Department). This is during official working hours, starting from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>), for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) only, seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (K-Net payment only) for the booklet. Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises are exempt from these fees (upon presentation of the relevant certificate). This will be effective from Sunday, 2/2/2025, from 8:00 AM until 1:00 PM, taking into account the following:
1- The deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on Thursday, 13/2/2025. No bids will be accepted after this time.
2- Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Tenders and Follow-up Department - Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> - Administrative Building - First Floor - Zone 7.
3- Submission of an initial security deposit of not less than (2%) of the bid value in favor of the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig>, in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check from one of the Kuwaiti banks, valid throughout the bid validity period of (90) days.
4- Submission of a valid national labor percentage compliance certificate.
5- A letter of authorization and a copy of the civil ID for the company representative to purchase the tender document.
6- This tender is indivisible, and alternative offers are not permitted.
7- The bidder must submit a letter accompanied by a copy of the registration certificate with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.

8- The preliminary meeting and site inspection will be on Sunday, 9/2/2025, at 11:00 AM. The bid must remain valid for a period of (90) days from the closing date, with the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> reserving its right to extend or renew this period for such duration(s) as it deems appropriate to complete the award procedures.
9- Companies must be registered with the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> (Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> website) /https://pnsd.da.gov.kw/ar.
This tender is subject to Circular No. (1) of 2023 regarding tenders in public entities.

For inquiries: Email: ad.alnassar@da.gov.kw
Direct: 22011424

## Announcement
### Public Practice Tender No. (DA/M/791)
The Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> announces a practice tender No. (DA/M/791) for the purchase of endpoint protection system licenses. Companies or institutions specialized in this field wishing to participate should apply to obtain the terms and conditions booklet and practice documents during official working hours from (Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> – Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7 – Tenders and Follow-up Department <orig>إدارة المناقصات والمتابعة</orig>), starting from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette (Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>), for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars only (K-Net payment only) per booklet, starting from Sunday, 2/2/2025, from 8:30 AM to 1:30 PM, taking into account the following:
1- The deadline for submitting bids is 1:30 PM on Sunday, 13/2/2025. No bids will be accepted after this time.
2- Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Tenders and Follow-up Department <orig>إدارة المناقصات والمتابعة</orig> – Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7.
3- Submission of an initial security deposit of 2% of the bid value in favor of the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check from one of the Kuwaiti banks, valid throughout the bid validity period of (90) days.
4- Submission of a valid national labor percentage compliance certificate and a tax compliance certificate.
5- A letter of authorization and a copy of the civil ID for the company representative to purchase the practice document.
6- This practice is indivisible, and alternative offers are not permitted.
7- The practitioner must submit a letter accompanied by a copy of the registration certificate with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.

The preliminary meeting is scheduled for Sunday, 9/2/2025, at 10:00 AM. The bid must remain valid for a period of (90) days from the closing date, with the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> reserving its right to extend or renew this period for such duration(s) as it deems appropriate to complete the award procedures.
For inquiries, please call the following numbers:
Direct: 22011427-22011437
Email: da.alnemash@da.gov.kw
Undersecretary for Financial, Administrative, and Personnel Affairs

The Public Authority for Minors' Affairs <orig>الهيئة العامة لشئون القصر</orig> announces its desire to issue practice tender No. (11-2024/2025) regarding cybersecurity and penetration testing assessment for the Public Authority for Minors' Affairs <orig>الهيئة العامة لشئون القصر</orig> for the year 2024/2025.

(fees payable via K-Net) at the following address: Al-Mirqab <orig>المرقاب</orig> – Abdullah Al-Mubarak Street <orig>شارع عبد الله المبارك</orig> – Next to the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> – Eighth Floor – Financial Department <orig>الإدارة المالية</orig>.

## Announcement of Practice Tender
### Practice No. T.M. - 2024/275-2028
**Development of Information Security Management System (ISMS)**

The General Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig> announces the tender for the above-mentioned practice. Specialized companies in this field, registered with the General Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig>, are requested to visit (Financial Affairs) (General Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig> Headquarters - Sharq <orig>شرق</orig> - Plot 1 - Street 201 - 21st Floor) to obtain the practice documents for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) (only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars), payable by certified check. The specifications booklet is to be delivered to (Information Technology Department <orig>إدارة تقنية المعلومات</orig>) (General Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig> Headquarters - Sharq <orig>شرق</orig> - Plot 1 - Street 201 - 26th Floor - Office No. (2611)).

Bids are to be submitted during official working hours starting from Sunday, 2/2/2025, with the last day for submission being Sunday, 2/23/2025. Bids must be delivered in sealed envelopes on the specified date before 1:00 PM (General Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig> Headquarters - Sharq <orig>شرق</orig> - Plot 1 - Street 201 - 22nd Floor - Room No. (2217)).

The practitioner must also attach the following documents with the bid:
- 1- Copy of the Commercial Register.
- 2- Copy of the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig> certificate.
- 3- Copy of the company's registration receipt with the General Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig>.

- 5- Copy of the registration receipt with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
- 6- Copy of the practice purchase receipt.
- 7- The preliminary guarantee for the practice, valued at (2%), must be attached to the bid in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee issued by one of the accredited banks in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> in favor of the General Investment Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للاستثمار</orig>, unconditional, and valid for at least (90) ninety days from the last date for receiving bids.
- 8- Attach a certificate of payment of subscriptions to the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> as stipulated in Article (95) of the Social Security Law <orig>قانون التأمينات الاجتماعية</orig>.
- 9- Attach a valid "To Whom It May Concern" certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file regarding government contracts registered with the private sector, noting that bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.

Acting Executive Director of Operations Sector

Announcement

The Public Authority for Sport / Al-Hay'a Al-Amma Lil-Riyadha <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> announces the offering of Practice No.: PASD (2024/2025/67) regarding landscaping works to specialized companies for performing landscaping in all club facilities in preparation for the annual visit of His Highness the Amir of the country during the blessed month of Ramadan at the Kuwait Sports Club for the Disabled / Nadi Al-Kuwait Al-Riyadhi Lil-Mu'aqeen <orig>نادي الكويت الرياضي للمعاقين</orig>, in sealed envelopes according to the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents, which can be obtained from the Services and Supplies Department – Tenders and Practices Section – Ground Floor, Office No. (5) at the Authority's headquarters in Al-Riqqa <orig>الرقعي</orig> area during official working hours or through the website of the Public Authority for Sport / Al-Hay'a Al-Amma Lil-Riyadha <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).

Deadline for closing the practice.
*   Practitioners must adhere to the instructions regarding submitting bids (CD) on the website of the Public Authority for Sport / Al-Hay'a Al-Amma Lil-Riyadha <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (Pas.gov.kw/tenders).
*   Companies / practitioners wishing to submit inquiries or clarifications, etc., must do so at the time and place specified above in the preliminary meeting schedule (inquiry session), and no inquiry will be considered after the deadline.
*   All documents must be submitted on a (CD) and a non-copyable hard copy, except for the bid form and the preliminary insurance, which must be submitted as a hard copy. Bids are valid for (90) ninety days from the date of opening bids. Any bid not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for purchasing the practice documents, the preliminary guarantee, and the national labor support certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower / Al-Hay'a Al-Amma Lil-Quwa Al-Amila <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> for the year 2025 will be excluded.
*   The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower / Al-Hay'a Al-Amma Lil-Quwa Al-Amila <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority or any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 8 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. Bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.
*   The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water, and Renewable Energy / Wizarat Al-Kahraba' wal-Ma' wal-Taqa wal-Taqa Al-Mutajaddida <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة والطاقة المتجددة</orig> stating clearance from consumption debts.
*   The practice is open to all companies and institutions specialized in the required works and registered with the Public Authority for Sport / Al-Hay'a Al-Amma Lil-Riyadha <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> and the Central Agency for Public Tenders / Al-Jihaz Al-Markazi Lil-Munakasat Al-Amma <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for the year 2025, for a fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> only, payable via K-Net (non-refundable except in cases stipulated by Ministry of Finance / Wizarat Al-Maliya <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> circulars), bringing the following:
    1.  A copy of the practice announcement in the Official Gazette.
    2.  A copy of the company's registration with the Authority for the year 2025.
    3.  A written letter of authorization approved by the Authority, accompanied by (a copy of the civil ID – a copy of the signature authorization).
*   Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises (SMEs) are exempt from the prescribed fees for purchasing practice documents in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016.

# Announcement of Public Practice No. / H.A.R.D. (2025/2024/68) Regarding Maintenance Works for Board of Directors Meeting Room Equipment

This is to be submitted in sealed envelopes in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the practice documents, which can be obtained from the Services and Supplies Department <orig>إدارة الخدمات والتوريدات</orig> – Tenders and Practices Section <orig>قسم المناقصات والممارسات</orig> – Ground Floor, Office No. (5) at the headquarters of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> in Al-Riqqa <orig>الرقعي</orig> area during official working hours or through the website (pas.gov.kw/tenders).

| Issue Date | Closing Date | Document Price | Initial Guarantee |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|

One Thousand Five Hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only, to be submitted as an original certified cheque or a letter of guarantee valid for (90) days and in favor of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> from the closing date. |
</table>

## Preliminary Meeting (Inquiry Session)

At 11:00 AM on Sunday, 2025/02/09, at the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> (Fifth Floor). No inquiries will be entertained after this time.

Bids must be submitted from 9:00 AM until 2:00 PM on the closing date. Bids must be delivered in sealed envelopes with red wax and placed in the box designated for practices at the Authority's headquarters (Ground Floor). No bids received after the specified closing time for the practice will be accepted.

- Practitioners must adhere to the instructions regarding the submission of bids (CD) on the website of the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig>.
- Practitioners wishing to submit any inquiries or clarifications regarding the advertised practice must attend at the time or place specified in the table above for the preliminary meeting (inquiry session). No inquiries will be entertained after this time.
- All documents must be submitted on a (CD) and a non-reproducible hard copy, except for the bid format and initial insurance, which must be submitted in hard copy. Furthermore,
- Bids shall be valid for (90) ninety days from the date of bid opening. Any bid not accompanied by the original or a copy of the receipt for purchasing the practice documents, the initial guarantee, and the national labor support certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> for the year 2025 will be excluded.
- The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file regarding government contracts registered with the Authority or any of the violations mentioned in Article (10) of Law No. 8 of 2010 concerning work in the private sector. Bids that do not include this certificate will be excluded.
- The bidder must attach a valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> stating clearance from consumption debts.

The practice is open to all companies and establishments specialized in the required works and registered with the Public Authority for Sport <orig>الهيئة العامة للرياضة</orig> and the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> for the year 2025, for a fee of (75 K.D.) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only, payable via K-Net (non-refundable except in cases stipulated by Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> circulars), bringing with them the following:

- 1- A copy of the practice announcement in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.
- 2- A copy of the company's registration with the Authority for the year 2025.
- 3- A written letter of authorization approved by the Authority, accompanied by (a copy of the Civil ID <orig>البطاقة المدنية</orig> – a copy of the signature authorization).
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> are exempted from the prescribed fees for purchasing practice documents, in accordance with the text of Article (39) of Law No. 74/2019 regarding amendments to Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. (49/2016).
- Owners of small and medium-sized enterprises <orig>المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> wishing to apply for the practice must attach a valid certificate issued by the National Fund for Small and Medium Enterprise Care and Development <orig>الصندوق الوطني لرعاية وتنمية المشروعات الصغيرة والمتوسطة</orig> stating their accreditation as a small or medium enterprise.
- In accordance with the text of Article (48) of Public Tenders Law <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig> No. (49) of (2016), which states: "Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the practice documents in a public session attended by the bidders or their representatives."
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested practitioners to attend, as interested companies have the right to coordinate with the competent committee before the session date to attend the bid opening session.

Announcement

Regarding the issuance of Purchase Order No. 8969
for the supply of Electrical cables

These documents can be obtained by visiting the website bids.pai.gov.kw starting from the date of publication of this announcement.
<table_caption>Tender Details for Electrical Cables</table_caption>
<table>
| Tender | Closing Date | Document Price | Initial Security Deposit | Preliminary Meeting |
|:------|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 2025/2/2 | 2025/2/13 | 75 K.D. | 150 K.D. | None. |

The deadline for submitting bids is Thursday, 2/13/2025, until 12:00 PM. Bids shall be submitted at the main headquarters of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> (Second Floor - Supplies and Warehouses Department - Procurement Section) in an envelope bearing the name of the practice. Bids shall be valid for a period of (90) days from the date of opening the bid envelopes.
The bidder must submit a recent 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> stating that there is no suspension on the company's file regarding government contracts registered with the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, and a 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate confirming compliance with the national labor percentage, dated recently and contemporary to the bid date. The bidder must also deposit with their bid an initial security deposit in the form of a certified check or an unconditional letter of guarantee issued by any bank operating in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> in favor of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> and valid for the duration of the bid. Any bid not accompanied by the full security deposit will be excluded. The initial security deposit may not be refunded until (90) days have passed from the closing date of the practice or when the winning bidder signs the contract, unless the practice is canceled. The Authority will not pay any interest on the amount of this security deposit, and the bidder's creditors may not seize its amount. Please note that this practice is indivisible.

Announcement

The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces the termination of the contractual relationship pertaining to the investment contract for the design, construction, management, operation, and maintenance of a crafts industries complex in the Al-Shuwaikh <orig>الشويخ</orig> Crafts, Industrial, and Commercial Area, allocated to Agility Public Warehousing Company <orig>شركة اجياليتي للمخازن العمومية</orig> for its utilization, due to the latter's unwillingness to renew.
Due to the termination of this relationship, the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> urges the esteemed occupants of shops at that location, under contracts previously concluded with the company, to cease dealing with it regarding those shops, with a warning that the Authority will not recognize any dealings with the company regarding those plots after 2/11/2024.

# Announcement

A company authorization must be presented for the person authorized to purchase the practice documents. Bids shall be placed in the designated box at the Authority's headquarters and shall be valid for a period of (90) days from the date of opening the bid envelopes. The bid must be accompanied by an initial guarantee of 2% of the bid value, which should be in the form of an accredited letter of guarantee or a certified check issued by one of the accredited local banks, and valid for the duration of the bid. Please note that this practice is indivisible, and alternative offers will not be accepted. The last deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on Monday, 17/2/2025.

## Public Anti-Corruption Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة لمكافحة الفساد</orig>
### Announcement Regarding the Receipt of Financial Disclosure Statements
The Public Anti-Corruption Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة لمكافحة الفساد</orig> (Nazaha <orig>نزاهة</orig>) calls upon those covered by the financial disclosure system to submit their declarations within the legal deadlines, in order to promote integrity and avoid legal penalties that may extend to imprisonment or dismissal from office.
Nazaha <orig>نزاهة</orig> also emphasizes the necessity of updating the declaration every three years for those who remain in their positions.
To find out the deadlines for submitting the declaration, to download financial disclosure forms, and to book an appointment in advance, please visit the Authority's website www.nazaha.gov.kw, call 118, or use the Sahel <orig>سهل</orig> platform.

# General Administration of Customs <orig>الإدارة العامة للجمارك</orig>
## Public Auction Announcement
The General Administration of Customs <orig>الإدارة العامة للجمارك</orig> announces that on Wednesday, 5/2/2025, at 11:00 AM, goods consisting of the following will be sold:

at the General Administration of Customs <orig>الإدارة العامة للجمارك</orig>, specifically at the headquarters of the Bait Al-Mal <orig>بيت المال</orig> Control Department, located in Al-Sulaibiya <orig>الصليبية</orig> on the Sixth Ring Road.
Therefore, those wishing to purchase should attend the auction site on the specified date, taking into account the following sales conditions:
1. The Auction Sales Committee <orig>لجنة البيع بالمزاد</orig> has the right to sell the goods in one lot or several lots, depending on the sales circumstances.
2. The successful bidder shall bear a brokerage commission of 2% of the sale price.
3. The successful bidder must pay the value of the goods only via K-net, according to the assessment of the Auction Sales Committee <orig>لجنة البيع بالمزاد</orig>.
4. The successful bidder must promptly remove the goods from the headquarters of the Bait Al-Mal <orig>بيت المال</orig> Control Department within 5 (five) to 7 (seven) days after the auction is awarded to them. Otherwise, any goods will be seized and sold in the next auction if the successful bidder fails to remove them within the specified period.
5. If the goods are not sold for any reason, the committee has the right to offer them for sale in the subsequent auction.
6. The Administration has the right to stop, postpone, or reschedule the sale at another time if a suitable price is not obtained or for any reasons it deems contrary to its interests.
7. The Auction Sales Committee <orig>لجنة البيع بالمزاد</orig> may cancel or postpone the auction for any reason it deems appropriate.
8. Since the goods will be sold as-is, bidders must inspect them to ascertain their condition, quality, and type, at the address mentioned above, during the auction sale.
9. In the event that the successful bidder refrains from paying the sale price or part thereof, the General Administration of Customs <orig>الإدارة العامة للجمارك</orig> has the right to resell the goods at their expense. If the price does not reach the amount for which the auction was initially awarded, they are obligated to pay the difference. In this case, the Administration has the right to bar them from participating in any future auctions.
10. The Administration is not responsible for any action or use of the sold goods that violates applicable laws and legislations.
11. This sale is conducted in accordance with the provisions of Law No. 10 of 2003 regarding the Unified Customs System <orig>النظام الموحد للجمارك</orig> and its regulating decisions.
12. All bidders must adhere to health and preventive requirements.
Auction Sales Committee <orig>لجنة البيع بالمزاد</orig>

Practice No. (34 - 2024/2025)
Managed Siem & DRP
The Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig> announces the offering of Practice No. (34-2024/2025) related to Managed SIEM & DRP at the Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>, in accordance with the terms and specifications mentioned in the practice documents, with adherence to scheduling appointments for government entities as per the esteemed Council of Ministers' <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig> decisions. These documents can be obtained from the Financial Affairs Department – Tenders and Contracts Section at the Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig> starting from Sunday, 2/2/2025, during official working hours, upon payment of an amount of (75 K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars, to be paid via K.net.
A preliminary meeting will be held at the headquarters of the Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig> on Sunday, 9/2/2025, at 11:00 AM.
The documents shall be returned after being filled out, with the required supporting documents attached, and an initial security deposit of no less than (2%) of the bid value, in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee issued by one of the accredited banks in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, issued in the name of the bidder and in favor of the Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>, and not subject to any restriction or condition. # Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig>
## Announcement
The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> announces its desire to issue Practice No. (8-2024/2025) for the renewal of licenses, maintenance of network application devices, load distribution, and technical support services. Specialized companies wishing to apply for this practice must observe the following:
1. The company must be registered with the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig>.
2. The applying company must have experience in this field prior to the issuance of this announcement, with proof thereof.
3. The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> will begin issuing the practice terms and conditions starting from the date of this announcement for a period of 10 days.
4. The practice terms and conditions can be obtained from the Financial Affairs Department <orig>إدارة الشئون المالية</orig> for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig>.
5. The preliminary meeting with the bidders will be held on Thursday, 6/2/2025, at 10:00 AM in the building of the General Secretariat of the Supreme Council for Planning <orig>الأمانة العامة للمجلس الأعلى للتخطيط</orig> – Second Floor.
6. Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Financial Affairs Department <orig>إدارة الشئون المالية</orig> of the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> no later than 1:00 PM on Thursday, 13/2/2025.

## Announcement

Specialized companies wishing to apply for this practice must observe the following:
1. The company must be registered with the Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig>.
2. The applying company must have experience in this field prior to the issuance of this announcement, with proof thereof.
3. The Central Statistical Bureau <orig>الإدارة المركزية للإحصاء</orig> will begin issuing the practice terms and conditions starting from the date of this announcement for a period of 10 days.
4. The practice terms and conditions can be obtained from the Financial Affairs Department <orig>إدارة الشئون المالية</orig> for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig>.

This is based on Article No. (18) of Public Tenders Law No. 49 of 2016 <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة رقم 49 لسنة 2016</orig>, Decision No. (51) of Meeting No. (2025/8). # National Cyber Security Center <orig>المركز الوطني للأمن السيبراني</orig>
## Award Announcement

The National Cyber Security Center <orig>المركز الوطني للأمن السيبراني</orig> announces the award of the following practices:

<table_caption>National Cyber Security Center Tender Awards</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Description | Subject |
|:--|:------|:--------|
| 1 | Practice No. 2025/2024 regarding Cyber Incident Response for the National Cyber Security Center <orig>المركز الوطني للأمن السيبراني</orig> | Awarded to Messrs. Al-Kharafi Computer Company <orig>شركة الخرافي للحاسبات</orig> for a total value of 74,850 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> – third lowest price after excluding the lowest prices due to non-compliance with technical terms and specifications. |
| 2 | Practice No. 2025/2024 regarding the project for design, hosting, and protection of the website and smart devices for the National Cyber Security Center <orig>المركز الوطني للأمن السيبراني</orig> | Awarded to Messrs. Sahab Integrated Computing Company <orig>شركة سحب للحاسوبية المتكاملة</orig> for a total value of 69,000 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> – second lowest price and compliant with technical specifications. |
</table>

For inquiries, please contact via email
aaljimaz@ncsc.gov.kw

# Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>
## Announcement 2025/12

The holder of the following licenses has applied to the Municipality:

<table_caption>Kuwait Municipality License Holder Details</table_caption>
<table>
| Commercial Name | Category | Registration No. |
|:---|:-----|:---------|
| Abdullah Saad Aaber General Trading and Contracting Company <orig>شركة عبد الله سعد عابر للتجارة العامة والمقاولات</orig> | Municipality Contractor, Category C | 2000536 |
</table>

Requests the release of the company's bank guarantees deposited with the Municipality in consideration of its classification.

Based on Article (19) of Municipality Resolution No. (2009/161) regarding the classification, licensing, and registration of building and demolition contractors in Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>, which stipulates that a contractor may submit an application to the Municipality to cancel their registration before its expiry or to cancel the classification, and the committee stipulated in Article One of this regulation may issue its decision thereon after fulfilling the following two conditions:
- The contractor has completed all contracted works.
- The lapse of fifteen (15) days from the date of publication of this application in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

The cancellation of the license or registration entails the return of the bank guarantee submitted by the contractor, taking into account the last paragraph of Article (10) of this resolution.
Accordingly, the Municipality appeals to anyone who has any claims against the aforementioned contractor regarding building contracts concluded between them that have not yet been completed, or judicial attachments against the owner due to violating contracting works or dues arising from the contracting agreement, to review the Contractors Section <orig>قسم المقاولين</orig> in the Engineering Systems Department <orig>إدارة الأنظمة الهندسية</orig> within a maximum period of fifteen days from this date. The Municipality will not consider any claims submitted after the prescribed period.

Director General of the Municipality

## Announcement No. 2025/14

Regarding the extension of the closing date for preparing the study and design by direct contract No. 5 for the project of methods to address the Al-Messilah <orig>المسيلة</orig> area coast, plots 7+6, from erosion and corrosion operations extending from Al-Messilah Village <orig>قرية المسيلة</orig> beach to Sabah Al-Salem Bridge <orig>جسر صباح السالم</orig> beach.

Further to the announcement published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> on 2024/12/22 regarding the direct contract No. 5 for preparing the study and design for the project of methods to address the Al-Messilah <orig>المسيلة</orig> area coast, plots 7+6, from erosion and corrosion operations extending from Al-Messilah Village <orig>قرية المسيلة</orig> beach to Sabah Al-Salem Bridge <orig>جسر صباح السالم</orig> beach, for which the closing date was set as 2025/1/27.

Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> announces the postponement of the closing date for direct contract No. 5 for preparing the study and design for the project of methods to address the Al-Messilah <orig>المسيلة</orig> area coast, plots 7+6, from erosion and corrosion operations extending from Al-Messilah Village <orig>قرية المسيلة</orig> beach to Sabah Al-Salem Bridge <orig>جسر صباح السالم</orig> beach, to become Monday, 2025/2/17.

Director General of the Municipality

## Announcement 2025/13
### Practice No. A-2025/2024-20
### Supply of Kuwait State Flags <orig>أعلام دولة الكويت</orig>

Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> announces the re-tender of Practice No. A-2025/2024-20 for the supply of Kuwait State Flags <orig>أعلام دولة الكويت</orig> in accordance with the general and special terms and specifications. Bids shall be submitted on the day of the auction, from 11:30 AM to 12:00 PM, on Wednesday, 2025/2/5, at Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> building (Financial Affairs Department <orig>إدارة الشئون المالية</orig> – Second Floor). No bids will be accepted after 12:00 PM.

1) Location for obtaining the terms and conditions booklet and submitting auction participation offers: (Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> Headquarters) Office of the Director of Financial Affairs Department <orig>إدارة الشئون المالية</orig>, from the date of announcement until February 5, 2025. Kuwait University <orig>جامعة الكويت</orig>
Announcement
Kuwait University <orig>جامعة الكويت</orig> announces the offering of the following divisible practices (tenders):

<table_caption>Kuwait University Tenders for Programs and Classroom Outfitting</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Practice No. | Subject | Requesting Entity | Sale Price | Initial Security Deposit Value | Closing Date |
|:--|:---|:--------|:---|:---------|:---|:---|
| 1 | 2024-2025/205 | Purchase of Software | Various Work Centers | 75 K.D. | 2% of Bid Value | 2025/02/18 |
| 2 | 2024-2025/509 | Supply, Installation, Operation, and Outfitting of Distance Learning Classrooms | E-Learning Center | 75 K.D. | 2% of Bid Value | 2025/02/18 |
</table>

1- Practice (tender) documents can be obtained starting from Sunday, February 2, 2025, and subsequent days during official working hours from the Procurement Department's <orig>إدارة المشتريات</orig> website (https://pur.ku.edu.kw).
2- The deadline for submitting bids is Tuesday, February 18, 2025, at 12:00 PM. Bids received after this deadline will not be considered. Bids will be opened in a public session.
3- Instructions for Practitioners (Bidders): -
- Bids must be submitted on optical discs (CDs), 3 copies, ensuring that all files have been correctly copied before depositing the discs in a sealed envelope. The copies must be identical, similar, and close to the original documents and stamped with the practitioner's (company's) seal.
- Inquiries are accepted within 10 days from the date of the announcement. No inquiries will be accepted after the specified deadline.
- The following paper documents must be submitted: -
  - The original copy of the bid form and undertaking.
  - Initial security deposit (as per the tender announcement).
  - Purchase receipt from the website.
  - A valid and acceptable copy of the national labor percentage certificate.
  - A valid 'To Whom It May Concern' certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, stating that there is no suspension on the practitioner's file.
  - Envelopes designated for the practice (tender).
- The bid will be disqualified if any document mentioned in the instructions is not submitted.
- Bids are to be placed in the designated box at the Procurement Department <orig>إدارة المشتريات</orig> – at Sabah Al-Salem University City <orig>مدينة صباح السالم الجامعية</orig> (Al-Shaddadiya <orig>الشدادية</orig>) – University Administration Building – Sixth Floor.
- Suppliers Affairs Section <orig>قسم شئون الموردين</orig>.
Note: -
- Tender documents are to be collected by companies specialized in this field, provided they are registered with the University's Suppliers Affairs Section <orig>قسم شئون الموردين</orig> and registered with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>, during official working hours.

# Abdullah Al-Salem University <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig>
## Announcement
### Tender Practice No. 2025-2024/21
**Supply and Installation of Carpets for Classrooms, Offices, and Theater**

<table_caption>Tender Details for Supply and Installation of Carpets (Practice No. 2025-2024/21)</table_caption>
<table>
| Submission | Closing | Price | Guarantee |
|:------|:--------|:------|:--------|
| 2/2/2025 | 2/16/2025 | 75 K.D. | 2% initial security for 90 days |
</table>

*   **Preliminary Meeting:** The preliminary meeting will be held on 2/9/2025, at 10:00 AM in the meeting room of the Facilities and Engineering Affairs Department, Building KH-3B, at the university's Al-Khalidiya <orig>الخالدية</orig> campus.
*   **Public Envelope Opening Meeting:** The meeting will be held on 2/16/2025 at 14:00 in the meeting room of the Procurement and Warehousing Department in Al-Khalidiya <orig>الخالدية</orig>, noting that the last deadline for submitting bids is 13:00 on the closing date at the university headquarters.

Abdullah Al-Salem University <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig> announces Tender Practice No. 2025-2024/21 regarding the supply and installation of carpets for classrooms, offices, and the theater, in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the (Practice Documents). These can be obtained from the Procurement and Warehousing Department in the university building (KH2 - Ground Floor), Gate No. (3) in Al-Khalidiya <orig>الخالدية</orig>, and payment is made via K-Net. Bids must include initial security, whether bank guarantees or certified bank checks, bearing the name of the submitting company or institution and the beneficiary, Abdullah Al-Salem University <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig>. A national labor support certificate must be attached with the bids, otherwise, the bid will be considered void.

Note: Follow Abdullah Al-Salem University's <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig> website aasu.edu.kw for any updates regarding Practice (2025-2024/21).

---

## Announcement
### Tender Practice No. 2025-2024/28
**Provision of Printed Textbooks for the Second Semester 2024/2025**

<table_caption>Tender Details for Provision of Printed Textbooks (Practice No. 2025-2024/28)</table_caption>
<table>
| Submission | Closing | Price | Guarantee |
|:------|:--------|:------|:--------|
| 2/3/2025 | 2/17/2025 | 75 K.D. | 2% initial security for 90 days |
</table>

*   **Preliminary Meeting:** None
*   **Public Envelope Opening Meeting:** The meeting will be held on 2/17/2025 at 14:00 in the meeting room of the Procurement and Warehousing Department in Al-Khalidiya <orig>الخالدية</orig>, noting that the last deadline for submitting bids is 13:00 on the closing date at the university headquarters.

Abdullah Al-Salem University <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig> announces Tender Practice No. 2025-2024/28 regarding the provision of printed textbooks for the second semester 2024/2025, in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the (Practice Documents). These can be obtained from the Procurement and Warehousing Department in the university building (KH2 - Ground Floor), Gate No. (3) in Al-Khalidiya <orig>الخالدية</orig>, and payment is made via K-Net. Bids must include initial security, whether bank guarantees or certified bank checks, bearing the name of the submitting company or institution and the beneficiary, Abdullah Al-Salem University <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig>. A national labor support certificate must be attached with the bids, otherwise, the bid will be considered void.

Note: Follow Abdullah Al-Salem University's <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig> website aasu.edu.kw for any updates regarding Practice (2025-2024/28).

---

## Announcement of Tender Practice No. 2025-2024/23
**Supply and Installation of Lecture Chairs for the Classrooms Building in Al-Khalidiya <orig>الخالدية</orig> (KH-53)**

Abdullah Al-Salem University <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig> announces Tender Practice No. 2025-2024/23 regarding the supply and installation of lecture chairs for the classrooms building in Al-Khalidiya <orig>الخالدية</orig> (KH-53), in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the (Practice Documents).

<table_caption>Tender Details for Supply and Installation of Lecture Chairs (Practice No. 2025-2024/23)</table_caption>
<table>
| Submission | Closing | Price | Guarantee |
|:------|:--------|:------|:--------|
| 2/2/2025 | 2/16/2025 | 75 K.D. | 2% initial security for 90 days |
</table>

*   **Preliminary Meeting:** The meeting will be held on 2/6/2025, at 10:00 AM in the meeting room of the Facilities and Engineering Affairs Department, Building KH-3B, at the university campus.

Note: Follow Abdullah Al-Salem University's <orig>جامعة عبدالله السالم</orig> website aasu.edu.kw for any updates regarding Practice (2025-2024/23).

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Competition Protection Authority Announcement <orig>إعلان جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig>",

}

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724, Seventy-First Year
121
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH – 2/2/2025
Competition Protection Authority <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig>
Announcement
</header>
The Competition Protection Authority <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig> announces the submission of a request by

<table_caption>Details of Parties Involved in Economic Concentration Request</table_caption>
<table>
| Party | Details |
|:------|:--------|
| **First Private Equity for General Trading Company (Single Person Company)** <orig>شركة الملكية الخاصة الأولى للتجارة العامة (شركة الشخص الواحد)</orig> <br> First Private Equity for General Trading Co. | **Activity:** Activities related to buying and selling shares and bonds solely for the company's account and utilizing the company's available financial surpluses. |
| **Taly Holding Limited (Private Company Limited by Shares) (Abu Dhabi)** <orig>شركة تالي القابضة المحدودة (شركة خاصة محدودة بالأسهم) (أبوظبي)</orig> <br> taly | **Activity:** Non-material holding company activities. |
</table>

for approval to complete an economic concentration process.
This involves the acquisition by First Private Equity for General Trading Company (Single Person Company) <orig>شركة الملكية الخاصة الأولى للتجارة العامة (شركة الشخص الواحد)</orig> of 65.7% of the shares of Taly Holding Limited (Private Company Limited by Shares) (Abu Dhabi) <orig>شركة تالي القابضة المحدودة (شركة خاصة محدودة بالأسهم) (أبوظبي)</orig>.
In accordance with Law No. (72) of 2020 regarding Competition Protection <orig>حماية المنافسة</orig> and Article (83) of its Executive Regulations issued by Board of Directors Resolution No. (14) of 2021, which stipulates that "any interested party may submit a reasoned objection to the Authority <orig>الجهاز</orig> regarding the economic concentration request within a period not exceeding (15) fifteen days from the date of notification or publication."
Accordingly, the Authority <orig>الجهاز</orig> invites any interested party to submit their reasoned objection to this economic concentration within a period not exceeding fifteen days from the date of this announcement.
Objection data should be submitted at the headquarters of the Competition Protection Authority <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig>, Al Hamra Tower <orig>برج الحمراء</orig>, 14th Floor, by filling out the form available on the website and paying the prescribed fee.

<footer>
<table_caption>Competition Protection Authority Contact Information</table_caption>
<table>
| Type | Details |
|:-----|:--------|
| Website | http://www.cpa.gov.kw |
| Email | info@cpa.gov.kw |
| Instagram | @cpakwt |
| Twitter | @cpa_kw |
| Phone | 22202274 |
| Fax | 22202261 |
</table>
</footer>

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm - Competition Protection Agency Announcement",
  "document_date": "2025-02-02",

}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724, Seventy-First Year
122
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
</header>
# Announcement

The Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig> announces the submission by

### Nabors Industries Limited <orig>شركة نابورس اندستريز ليمتد</orig> (United States of America)
Activity: Management and operation of drilling services, pipe running services, and fabrication workshop services.

<image_caption>Nabors Industries Limited Logo</image_caption>
<image>
{
  "description": "Logo of Nabors Industries, featuring a stylized 'N' and the company name 'NABORS'",
  "type": "logo",
  "data": "NABORS"
}
</image>

### Parker Drilling Company <orig>شركة باركر دريلينج</orig> (United States of America)
Activity: Management and operation of drilling services, pipe running services, and fabrication workshop services.

<image_caption>Parker Wellbore Logo</image_caption>
<image>
{
  "description": "Logo of Parker Wellbore, featuring a stylized 'P' and the company name 'PARKER WELLBORE' with the slogan 'Energy. Well engineered.'",
  "type": "logo",
  "data": "PARKER WELLBORE Energy. Well engineered."
}
</image>

of a request for approval to complete an economic concentration process

through the acquisition of Parker Drilling Company <orig>شركة باركر دريلينج</orig> by Nabors Industries Limited <orig>شركة نابورس اندستريز ليمتد</orig> via the merger of Nabors Sub A <orig>نابورس سب ايه</orig>, a subsidiary wholly owned by Nabors Industries Limited <orig>شركة نابورس اندستريز ليمتد</orig>, with Parker Drilling Company <orig>شركة باركر دريلينج</orig>, such that Parker Drilling Company <orig>شركة باركر دريلينج</orig> will be the surviving entity after the merger.

In accordance with Law No. (72) of 2020 regarding Competition Protection <orig>حماية المنافسة</orig> and Article (83) of its Executive Regulations issued by Resolution No. (14) of 2021 and its amendments, which stipulates that "any interested party may submit a reasoned objection to the Agency regarding the economic concentration request within a period not exceeding (15) fifteen days from the date of notification or publication..."

Accordingly, the Agency invites any interested party to submit their reasoned objection to this economic concentration within a period not exceeding fifteen days from the date of this announcement.

Objection data should be submitted at the headquarters of the Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig>, Al Hamra Tower <orig>برج الحمراء</orig>, 14th Floor, by filling out the form available on the website and paying the prescribed fee.

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724, Seventy-First Year
123
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH / 2/2/2025 AD
</header>
# Announcement

The Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig> announces the submission by:

<table_caption>Details of Entities in Economic Concentration</table_caption>
<table>
| Entity Name | Activity | Logo/Notes |
|:---|:---------|:---|
| Warba Bank (K.S.C.P.) <orig>بنك وربة (ش.م.ك.ع)</orig> | Practicing all banking activities. | (See Warba Bank Logo below) |
| Al-Ghanim Commercial Company (W.L.L.) <orig>شركة الغانم التجارية (ذ.م.م)</orig> | Wholesale and retail trade. | No logo |
</table>

<image_caption>Warba Bank Logo</image_caption>
<image>
{
  "description": "Warba Bank logo with Arabic and English text",
  "type": "logo",
  "data": "WARBA BANK"
}
</image>

of a request for approval to complete an economic concentration process.

The acquisition by Warba Bank (K.S.C.P.) <orig>بنك وربة (ش.م.ك.ع)</orig> of all shares of Al-Ghanim Commercial Company (W.L.L.) <orig>شركة الغانم التجارية (ذ.م.م)</orig>, which owns 32.75% of the shares of Gulf Bank (K.S.C.P.) <orig>بنك الخليج (ش.م.ك.ع)</orig>.

In accordance with Law No. (72) of 2020 regarding Competition Protection <orig>حماية المنافسة</orig> and Article (83) of its Executive Regulations issued by Resolution No. (14) of 2021 and its amendments, which stipulates that "any interested party may submit a reasoned objection to the Agency <orig>الجهاز</orig> regarding the economic concentration request within a period not exceeding (15) fifteen days from the date of notification or publication..."

Accordingly, the Agency <orig>الجهاز</orig> invites all interested parties to submit their reasoned objections to this economic concentration within a period not exceeding fifteen days from the date of this announcement.

Objection data should be submitted at the headquarters of the Competition Protection Agency <orig>جهاز حماية المنافسة</orig>, Al Hamra Tower <orig>برج الحمراء</orig>, 14th Floor, by filling out the form available on the website, along with paying the prescribed fee.

<header>

Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1724 Seventy-First Year
</header>
# General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig>

## Tender Announcement No. (10-2024/2025)
### Design and Supervision Works for the Rapid Reaction Force Building Project at Al-Sumoud Camp <orig>معسكر الصمود</orig>

Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
For any inquiries, please call the switchboard at (24999999), extension 66734.

<table_caption>Tender Details for Project 66734</table_caption>
<table>
| Submission | Closing Date | Initial Security Deposit | Final Security Deposit |
|:------|:---|:---|:---|
| 2/2/2025 | 3/24/2025 at 1:00 PM sharp | K.D. 4,800/- <orig>د.ك</orig> valid for 90 days | (10%) of the total contract value plus (90) days after contract execution |
</table>

The General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig> announces a special tender for the design and supervision works of the Rapid Reaction Force Building Project at Al-Sumoud Camp <orig>معسكر الصمود</orig>, open to offices (Category Two) qualified by the National Guard <orig>الحرس الوطني</orig> as listed in the table below, in accordance with the conditions stated in the tender documents.

<table_caption>List of Qualified Offices - Category Two</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Company/Establishment Name |
|:--|:---|
| 1 | Dar Al-Turath Engineering Consultants <orig>دار التراث للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
| 2 | Dar MEC Engineering Consultants <orig>دار إم إي سي للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
| 3 | Dar Osama Boukhamseen Engineering Consultants <orig>دار أسامة بوخمسين للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
| 4 | Dar The Kuwaiti Engineering Group <orig>دار المجموعة الهندسية الكويتية</orig> |
| 5 | Arab Consultants Engineering Office <orig>مكتب المستشارون العرب للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
| 6 | Dar Al-Khaleej Engineering Consultants <orig>دار الخليج للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
| 7 | Dar Mohammed Marwi Al-Hadiya Engineering Consultants <orig>دار محمد مروي الهدية للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
| 8 | Dar Jassim Qazard Engineering Consultants <orig>دار جاسم قازرد للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
</table>

Therefore, offices wishing to participate in the tender must register on the official website of the General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig> (www.kng.gov.kw) to purchase the tender documents for a non-refundable fee of (K.D. 150/-) <orig>د.ك</orig> (one hundred and fifty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only). Payment is to be made through the national electronic website using the (K-NET) service.

A preliminary meeting will be held on Monday, 2/10/2025, at 10:00 AM, at the General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig> building – Al-Riqqa'i <orig>الرقعي</orig> – Colonel Faisal Al-Jareed <orig>فيصل الجريد</orig> Building. Whether the bidder attends or not, they will be bound by all decisions, recommendations, or clarifications made during the meeting.

## Tender Announcement No. (11-2024/2025)
### Design and Supervision Works for the Technical Workshops Centers Project for Military Personnel Services at Al-Sumoud <orig>الصمود</orig> and Al-Tahrir <orig>التحرير</orig> Camps

The General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig> announces a special tender for the design and supervision works of the Technical Workshops Centers Project for Military Personnel Services at Al-Sumoud <orig>الصمود</orig> and Al-Tahrir <orig>التحرير</orig> Camps, open to offices (Category One B) qualified by the National Guard <orig>الحرس الوطني</orig> as listed in the table below, in accordance with the conditions stated in the tender documents.

<table_caption>List of Qualified Offices - Category One (B)</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Company/Establishment Name |
|:--|:---|
| 1 | Dar Nizar Al-Anjari Engineering Consultants <orig>دار نزار العنجري للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
| 2 | Dar Al-Habashi Engineering Consultants <orig>دار الحبشي للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
| 3 | Dar Al-Kuwait Technical Consultants <orig>دار الكويت للاستشارات الفنية</orig> |
| 4 | Dar Mubarak Fahad Al-Duwailah Engineering Consultants and Project Management <orig>دار مبارك فهد الدويلة للاستشارات الهندسية وإدارة المشاريع</orig> |
| 5 | Dar Al-Jazeera Engineering Consultants <orig>دار استشارات الجزيرة للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
| 6 | Dar The Joint Engineering Office for Engineering Consultants <orig>دار المكتب الهندسي المشترك للاستشارات الهندسية</orig> |
</table>

Therefore, offices wishing to participate in the tender must register on the official website of the General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig> (www.kng.gov.kw) to purchase the tender documents for a non-refundable fee of (K.D. 300/-) <orig>د.ك</orig> (three hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only). Payment is to be made through the national electronic website using the (K-NET) service.

A preliminary meeting will be held on Tuesday, 2/11/2025, at 10:00 AM, at the General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig> building – Al-Riqqa'i <orig>الرقعي</orig> – Colonel Faisal Al-Jareed <orig>فيصل الجريد</orig> Building. Whether the bidder attends or not, they will be bound by all decisions, recommendations, or clarifications made during the meeting. Furthermore, participating offices must print the minutes of the preliminary meeting from the official website of the General Presidency of the National Guard <orig>الرئاسة العامة للحرس الوطني</orig> (www.kng.gov.kw).

Note:
Offices wishing to attend the preliminary tender meeting must provide us with a colored copy of the civil ID of the authorized person attending, sent to the following email: TENDERS@KNG.GOV.KW, to arrange an entry permit. This must be done five working days before the meeting, specifically before 10:00 AM, accompanied by a letter of authorization from the company to attend the meeting and the purchase receipt.

|:------|:---|:---|:---|

|       | at 1:00 PM sharp | valid for 90 days | |
</table>
