## Announcement

The Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> announces the offering of Practice No. (PIFSS / P / 26 / 2024) for the purchase of an MDR monitoring and surveillance system, and for purchasing the practice documents and obtaining the compact disc (C.D) related to the practice. Attendance is at the main headquarters of the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> located in Al-Mirqab <orig>المرقاب</orig> area – Al-Sour <orig>السور</orig> Street – and by calling phone number (22994469 or 22994467).

<table_caption>Tender Details and Initial Insurance Value</table_caption>
<table>
| Offer Date | Closing Date | Purchase Fees | Initial Insurance Value |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 2025-02-02 | 2025-02-16 | 75 K.D. | 1,500 K.D. (One thousand five hundred Kuwaiti Dinars only) valid for (90) days |
| 2025-2-2 | 2025-3-2 | 750 K.D. | Item One: 750 K.D. (Seven hundred and fifty Kuwaiti Dinars) valid for (90) days<br>Item Two: 750 K.D. (Seven hundred and fifty Kuwaiti Dinars) valid for (90) days |
| Preliminary Meeting (Inquiry Session) | None | | |
</table>

1.  The aforementioned cash payment must be made only via "K-Net" at the Corporation's treasury.
2.  Bids must be submitted at the main headquarters of the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> – Al-Mirqab <orig>المرقاب</orig> – in the bid box located on the ground floor. The deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM.
3.  To submit any reservations or inquiries regarding the aforementioned practice, please send them to the following email address no later than Sunday, 16-2-2025. Requests submitted after this date will not be considered. Procurement@pifss.gov.kw
4.  The right to attend the preliminary meeting – if any – is restricted to companies participating in the practice, provided they bring an official letter from the practitioner authorizing the representative to attend the meeting, a copy of their civil ID, and a copy of the practice document purchase receipt.

The following documents must be submitted when purchasing the practice documents:
1.  An authorization letter from the company containing the name and civil ID number of the authorized person purchasing the practice documents.
2.  A copy of the civil ID of the authorized person purchasing the practice documents.

Furthermore, copies of the following documents must be enclosed inside the bid envelope:
1.  A recent copy of the company's license from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
2.  A recent copy of the registration certificate with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
3.  A recent copy of the certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>.
4.  A recent copy of the registration certificate with the Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig>.
5.  A recent clearance certificate stating that there are no suspension codes on the practitioner's file with the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, addressed to the Corporation and specific to the practice being offered.
6.  A certificate of payment of subscriptions to the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig>.
7.  A copy of the practitioner's registration form in the Suppliers, Contractors, and Vendors Register at the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> for the year the practice is offered.

# General Fire Force / Kuwait Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>
## Announcement of a Practice Tender
The General Fire Force / Kuwait Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig> announces the floating of Practice Tender No. (2025/2024/26) for the supply, installation, and maintenance of a fire debris inspection and analysis device.
Specialized traders in this field are requested to visit the Revenue Department (Cashier) at the General Fire Force / Kuwait Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig> in Mubarak Al-Abdullah <orig>مبارك العبدالله</orig> area - Second Floor, to obtain the specifications for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, bringing with them the following documents:
1.  Copy of the Commercial Register.
2.  Copy of the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig> certificate.
3.  Copy of the registration receipt with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
4.  Copy of the certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage for non-governmental companies, issued by the Ministry of Social Affairs and Labor <orig>وزارة الشئون الاجتماعية والعمل</orig> and valid for one year with the bid.
5.  Insurance value: 2% of the submitted bid value.
6.  Copy of the supplier registration receipt with the General Fire Force / Kuwait Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>.
7.  A preliminary meeting will be held on Tuesday, 11/2/2025, at 10:00 AM in Mubarak Al-Abdullah <orig>مبارك العبدالله</orig> area - West Mishref <orig>غرب مشرف</orig> - First Floor - Meeting Room of the Supplies and Stores Controller.
8.  Bids are to be submitted to the Tenders and Contracts Preparation Department at the General Fire Force / Kuwait Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig> in Mubarak Al-Abdullah <orig>مبارك العبدالله</orig> area (West Mishref <orig>غرب مشرف</orig>) - First Floor.
Please note that the deadline for submitting offers is Sunday, 3/2/2025, at 1:00 PM, at the Tenders and Contracts Preparation Department in Mubarak Al-Abdullah <orig>مبارك العبدالله</orig> area (West Mishref <orig>غرب مشرف</orig>) - First Floor.

Director of Financial Affairs Department

# Announcement
## Regarding the Collection of Fees on Grievances Submitted to the Board of Directors of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> Against Procedures and Decisions of the High Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig>

The High Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> for tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries announces, based on Resolution No. (3) of 2025 issued by the Chief Executive Officer of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig>, the collection of fees on grievances submitted to the Corporation's Board of Directors regarding procedures and decisions issued by the High Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig>, as follows:

*   Companies submitting grievances to the Board of Directors of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> are required to pay grievance fees, according to the estimated tender value as shown in the table below:

<table_caption>Grievance Fees for Kuwait Petroleum Corporation Tenders</table_caption>
<table>
| Service | Service Summary | Fee |
|:---|:---|:---|
| Grievance Requests | Estimated tender value from KWD 75,000 to KWD 1 million | KWD 1,000 |
| | Estimated tender value exceeding KWD 1 million up to KWD 10 million | KWD 2,000 |
| | Estimated tender value exceeding KWD 10 million up to KWD 100 million | KWD 3,000 |
| | Estimated tender value exceeding KWD 100 million | KWD 5,000 |
</table>

*   Fees are collected from companies submitting grievances to the Board of Directors through a deposit receipt into the Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> account mentioned below:
    -Account number: 1000482330
    -IBAN number: KW37NBOK0000000000001000482330
    -Account name: Kuwait Petroleum Corporation
    -Currency: KWD
    -Bank Name: National Bank of Kuwait, Head office branch

*   According to the prevailing rules, fees will be refunded if the grievance is accepted both formally and substantively.

Pursuant to the text of Article (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 regarding Public Tenders: "It is not permissible for one person or a group of persons acting jointly to register under more than one name during classification, or to submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions allow their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent with its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may, during classification, register himself and register each of his independent companies. The bid of a tenderer who violates this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law."
1- This tender is limited and indivisible.
2- This tender is conducted in a single stage, and bids must include the preliminary security deposit.
3- This tender is restricted to the companies listed in the table below, numbering (53) companies. Any company declining to submit a bid for this tender must inform Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية لتزويد الطائرات بالوقود</orig> via an official letter stating the reasons for declining to submit its bid, no later than the aforementioned closing date, to avoid not being invited to future tender practices of Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية لتزويد الطائرات بالوقود</orig>.

# Kuwait Ports Authority <orig>مؤسسة الموانئ الكويتية</orig>
## Announcement
### Regarding the Extension of Registration in the Bidders' Register
Kuwait Ports Authority <orig>مؤسسة الموانئ الكويتية</orig> announces the extension of the registration period in the Bidders' Register. Those wishing to register must submit their applications addressed to Mr./ Director General <orig>مدير عام</orig> of the Authority, and the applications must include the following information and documents:
1. Commercial Name of the Bidder.
2. Type of activity practiced by the Bidder.
3. Commercial Registration Number.
4. Date of Establishment.
5. Value of Paid-up Capital (according to official documents).
6. Address of the Head Office and locations of main branches.
7. Phone number, fax number, and email address.
Location for Submitting Applications:
Applications are to be submitted manually to the General Register Control at the Authority's headquarters located in Shuwaikh <orig>الشويخ</orig> area - Jamal Abdel Nasser Street <orig>شارع جمال عبد الناصر</orig> - 8th Floor, Ports Complex.
Important Notes:
The application conditions stated in the previous announcement published in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>), Issue 1719, Seventy-First Year, Page 233, dated 29/12/2024, have been amended as follows:
"Applications from companies listed on the blacklist of Kuwait Ports Authority <orig>مؤسسة الموانئ الكويتية</orig>, or companies against which final judicial rulings have been issued, will not be accepted."
Application Period:
The period for receiving applications is open.
Kuwait Ports Authority <orig>مؤسسة الموانئ الكويتية</orig>

### 4- Overview of the Tender Works:
This project includes Engineering, Procurement, and Construction (EPC) works for two (2) Airside Operation Facilities (AOF) for Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company (KAFCO <orig>شركة الكويت لتزويد الطائرات بالوقود</orig>), including fuelling facilities, unloading and loading facilities, storage, and pumping facilities within the airside area and near Terminal 2.

### 5- The tender closing date is at 1:00 PM on Tuesday, 4 March 2025 AD. Bids must be submitted at the Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية لتزويد الطائرات بالوقود</orig> building, and no bids will be accepted after the specified deadline.

### 6- The validity period for the preliminary bond is ninety (90) days from the closing date.

### 7- The preliminary meeting will be held at 11:00 AM on Thursday, 13 February 2025 AD. The meeting will take place at the headquarters of Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية لتزويد الطائرات بالوقود</orig> – Basement – Meeting Room.

### 8- The final deadline for submitting any inquiries, reservations, or requests by participating companies regarding this tender is 16 February 2025 AD. No such requests will be considered for any reason after this specified deadline.

### 9- The final time for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on the day specified in the above announcement for depositing bids. Bids shall be deposited in a sealed envelope in the special bid box located at the headquarters of Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية لتزويد الطائرات بالوقود</orig>, Basement floor –

### 10- The cost of purchasing the document is (KWD 500/-) five hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.

### 11- Documents are to be purchased via bank deposit into the account of Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية لتزويد الطائرات بالوقود</orig>, with the tender number and the name of the purchasing company clearly indicated on the bank purchase receipt, according to the following details:
Account No.: 1000407591
IBAN No.: KW02 NBOK 0000 0000 0000 1000407591
SWIFT: NBOKKWKW
To be submitted with the bid:
1- A preliminary bond in the form of a certified cheque or a letter of guarantee from a bank accredited in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, issued in the name of the bidder and in favor of Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية لتزويد الطائرات بالوقود</orig>, for the amount of (KWD 50,000) fifty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only.

Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company
Announcement
The Higher Procurement Committee (HPC) of Kuwait Petroleum Company (KPC), based on the request from Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company (KAFCO), announces the issuance of Limited Tender No. 23-24/23 regarding EPC of 2 AOF's and Associated Facilities.

<table_caption>Tender Details and Key Dates</table_caption>
<table>
| Issuance Date | Pre-Tender Meeting and last day for purchasing Tender Document | Closing Date | Purchasing Doc Fees | Bid Bond Value |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 02/02/2025    | 13/02/2025 | 04/03/2025   | KD 500 | KD 50,000      |
</table>

According to Article (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning public tenders' law, "No individual or group of individuals jointly may register under more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids if allowed by the tender conditions. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each with its own legal personality, financial status, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may register himself and each of his independent companies separately during classification. Any bid violating this article is considered void."

1. This Tender is limited and Not Subject to Split.
2. The Tender is limited, single-stage, and requires submission of bids with the Bid Bond.

3. The Tender is limited to the (53) companies listed in the table below. Companies that choose not to submit a bid must inform KAFCO via an official letter stating the reasons for withdrawal by the closing date mentioned above, to avoid exclusion from future KAFCO tenders.
4. Tender Scope: This project involves Engineering, Procurement and Construction (EPC of two (2 Nos.) Airside Operation Facility (AOF) of Kuwait Aviation Fuelling Company (KAFCO) including the fuel supply facilities, unloading and loading, storage and pumping facilities inside airside area and in the vicinity of T2.
5. The Tender closing date is 04/03/2025 at 1:00 PM. Bids must be submitted at KAFCO's headquarters. Late submissions will not be accepted.
6. The Bid Bond must remain valid for 90 days from the closing date.
7. The pre-tender meeting will be held on 13/02/2025 at 11:00 AM at KAFCO's headquarters, basement – meeting room.
8. The deadline for submitting any inquiries, reservations, or requests by participating companies regarding this Tender is 16/02/2025. No requests will be considered after this date.
9. The final time for bid submission is 1:00 PM on the designated closing date, as indicated above. Bids should be deposited in the designated bid box located at KAFCO's headquarters, basement floor.
10. The document purchase fee is 500/- KWD.
11. Document purchases should be made via bank transfer to KAFCO's account, with the tender number and purchasing company name clearly stated on the bank receipt, according to the following details:
    *   Account No.: 1000407591
    *   IBAN: KW02 NBOK 0000 0000 0000 1000407591
    *   SWIFT: NBOKKWKW

Bid Submission Requirements:
1. An Bid Bond in the form of a certified check or bank guarantee from a bank accredited in Kuwait, issued in the name of the bidder and payable to KAFCO, in the amount of 1,000 KWD.
2. Compliance with the contract scope and/or

# Kuwait Integrated Petroleum Industries Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للصناعات البترولية المتكاملة</orig> (KIPIC)
## Announcement
Kuwait Integrated Petroleum Industries Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للصناعات البترولية المتكاملة</orig> (KIPIC) – one of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> companies – announces the offering of Public Tender No. (CZ/GS/120)
The subject of which is: [Supply, Installation, Maintenance and Reallocation of Office Furniture at Company Offices]
Supply, installation, maintenance, and reallocation of office furniture for the company's employees in accordance with the general and specific terms and specifications contained in the public tender documents. The documents for this public tender can be obtained through the KIPIC K-Tendering Portal on our website: (https://ktendering.com.kw/)

*   Pre-bid Meeting: 2/16/2025 at 10:00 AM (10:00 AM) at Kuwait Integrated Petroleum Industries Company (KIPIC) <orig>الشركة الكويتية للصناعات البترولية المتكاملة</orig>, Commercial Group Building, Al-Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig>.
*   Please note that the deadline for submitting bids is Tuesday, 3/18/2025, at 1:00 PM (1:00 PM) local time for the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, and bids must be submitted through the KIPIC K-Tendering Portal mentioned above.
*   This tender is public and indivisible.
*   The bidder must meet the following conditions:
    1.  Number of years since establishment:
    *   A minimum of 3 years since establishment must be available, otherwise the application will be rejected.
    2.  Local Contractors:
    *   Contracts completed within the last ten years, with the cumulative value of previous contracts not less than KWD 516,000, and the minimum value of each contract not less than KWD 172,000.
    *   In the case of an ongoing contract:
    *   Only one contract will be considered, and the project completion rate in the contract must be 75%, supported by a letter from the client clarifying this and indicating the contractor's good performance. For this condition to be considered, at least two completed contracts must be available.
    *   Foreign Contractors:
    *   Contracts completed within the last ten years, with the cumulative value of contracts not less than KWD 630,700, and the minimum value of each completed contract not less than KWD 172,000.
    *   At least one completed contract outside the country of origin must be available for foreign applicants, and ongoing contracts will not be considered for calculating the cumulative value.
*   General Notes:
    *   All contracts must be a primary scope of work or have a part of the primary scope of work related to the supply and installation of office furniture.
    *   All contracts must have been executed with government entities, the oil and gas sector, the energy sector, or any related industrial facility projects, or projects of a general or private nature (such as shopping malls, high-rise buildings, hospitals, etc.), or in the banking sectors.
    *   Compliance with the requirements of the tender documents.
    *   Registration in the KIPIC K-Tendering Portal.

(https://ktendering.com.kw/)
*   All required documents and certificates must be attached to the bid through the KIPIC K-Tendering Portal as specified in the tender documents.
*   To register and obtain a username and password to access the KIPIC K-Tendering Portal, please contact the help phone numbers 23887792 / 23887793 / 23887794 or E-Mail: cwphelp@knpc.com.kw
*   Illustrative guidelines on how to submit a bid through the KIPIC K-Tendering Portal are available on our website.

**Environmental Monitoring & Laboratory Services for Al-Zour Refinery, LNGI and Associated Facilities**

Based on the approval of the Higher Purchasing Committee for tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries, at its meeting No. (2025/09) held on 1/22/2025, Kuwait Integrated Petroleum Industries Company (KIPIC) <orig>الشركة الكويتية للصناعات البترولية المتكاملة</orig> announces the award of the above tender to the bid submitted by M/s. ### Extension

8. The investment applicant must submit the following documents:
- A valid copy of the civil ID for the license holder.
- A valid copy of the commercial license for the offered activity.
- A labor census from the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> indicating the presence of actual labor for the submitted license.

- Memorandum of Association <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig>... etc., including previous experience when submitting the bid,
- Signing and submitting the declaration and undertaking form attached to the terms and conditions booklet.
- The terms and conditions booklet must be completed, signed, and stamped by the company and by the investor applying for investment.
- For inquiries and clarifications, please send an email to real.estate@pumc.com.kw from the date of offering the bids.

The documents shall be returned after being filled, stamped, and accompanied by the required documents and the initial guarantee of (K.D. 2,000) (two thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only) by certified check or a bank guarantee letter of the same value. Bids not accompanied by this security will not be considered, even if they conform to specifications. Documents must be submitted in an official envelope sealed with red wax and placed in the company's box by the specified deadline.
Please note that the final deadline for submitting bids is Thursday, 2/13/2025, at 12:00 PM.
It is also noted that a preliminary meeting was held on Thursday, 1/23/2025, at 10:00 AM at the company's headquarters.
This tender is restricted to companies and establishments specialized in these works, with the obligation to submit the company's/establishment's papers and documents (Memorandum of Association <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> - License - Authorized Signatories <orig>اعتمادات التوقيع</orig>... etc.), including previous experience for the last five years in the same field when submitting the bid, in accordance with the requirements mentioned in the general conditions of the tender, along with the obligation to provide proof of compliance with the National Labor Support Law <orig>قانون دعم العمالة الوطنية</orig>.
Secretary

## Announcement

The Public Facilities Management Company <orig>شركة إدارة المرافق العمومية</orig> announces the offering of tenders numbers (4 - 5 / P.F.M.C. / 2025/02) for the investment of two commercial shops, numbers (101 - 134), for the activity of "Gold and Jewelry Sales" on the first floor - Kuwait Central Gold and Jewelry Market <orig>سوق الكويت المركزي للذهب والمجوهرات</orig> building - in Al-Mubarakiya <orig>المباركية</orig> area, within the expatriate labor city <orig>مدينة العمالة الوافدة</orig> in Al-Shaddadiya <orig>الشدادية</orig> area.

<table_caption>Tender Details for Gold and Jewelry Shops in Kuwait Central Market</table_caption>
<table>
| Shop No. | Activity             | Automated No. | Area     | Minimum Investment Value |
|:---------|:---------------------|:--------------|:---------|:-------------------------|
| 101      | Gold and Jewelry Sales | 10188086      | 15.51 m2 | 310 K.D. / -             |
| 134      | Gold and Jewelry Sales | 10188481      | 14.66 m2 | 293 K.D. / -             |
</table>

This is according to the following conditions:
1. The announcement form, the declaration and undertaking form, and the required documents are considered an integral part of the terms and conditions booklet and an accompanying document to the bidding conditions.
2. The applicant must be a specialist and possess a valid commercial license matching the required license activity, to be submitted with the required documents. The applicant must be actively engaged in the activity through the presence of actual labor (not estimated labor) under the submitted license. The commercial license must be signed and stamped after verification and confirmation of compliance. The Internal Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء الداخلية</orig> wishes to draw the attention of practitioners who have inquiries or reservations regarding the technical specifications to submit such requests a maximum of (two weeks) before the closing date (for this practice). These requests will be rejected and will not be considered for any reason after this deadline.

# Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig>
## Announcement
The Internal Purchasing Committee of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> - one of the subsidiaries of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> - announces the offering of Practice No.: MAA-DC Emergency - RFQ/1054142 AGRP I - Shutdown Valve, in accordance with the general and special terms and conditions stipulated in the practice documents. These documents can be obtained by visiting the unified e-Tendering portal (K-Tendering portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries ((https://ktendering.com.kw)).

<table_caption>Tender Details for RFQ/1054142</table_caption>
<table>
| Offering Date | Preliminary Meeting | Closing Date | Initial Security |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 2/2/2025 | Not Applicable | 2/27/2025 | KWD 1,000 <orig>1,000 د.ك</orig> valid for (90) days |
</table>

The deadline for submitting bids is Thursday, 2/27/2025, at 1:00 PM local time in the State of Kuwait (13:00 Noon), noting that bids must be submitted through the e-Tendering portal mentioned above.
- The practitioner must submit the initial security in favor of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> in an envelope clearly marked with the name and address of the practice and the closing date. It must be placed in the designated box located on the first floor, reception hall, at the Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>الشركة الوطنية الكويتية</orig> Head Office building in Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig>, no later than 1:00 PM (13:00 Noon) on Thursday, 2/27/2025, along with a copy of the initial security for the bid.
- Please note that this practice is indivisible, and supply must be from the unified qualification list of the Central Qualification Committee mentioned in the practice documents.
- No single person or group of persons acting jointly may register under more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission.
- However, a person who has an interest in separate companies, each independent with its own legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may, during classification, register himself and each of his independent companies.
- Any bid from a tenderer violating these provisions shall be deemed null and void by operation of law, in accordance with Article No. (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning Public Tenders.
- Note: -
- All required documents and certificates must be attached to the bid through the e-Tendering portal, as specified in the practice documents.

## Auction Announcement
Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> announces the offering of Public Auction No. GS/AUC/019: Auction for the investment of designated spaces to provide direct sales locations in buildings belonging to Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig>, in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the auction documents, which can be obtained by visiting the unified e-Tendering portal (K-Tendering portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries: ((https://ktendering.com.kw)).
Please note that the deadline for submitting bids is Thursday, 4/17/2025, at 1:00 PM local time in the State of Kuwait (13:00 PM), and bids must be submitted through the e-Tendering portal mentioned above.
- The bidder must submit an initial security deposit of KWD 1,000 <orig>1000 د.ك</orig> (One Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars), valid for 90 days, in favor of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية</orig>. This must be in an envelope clearly marked with the name and address of the auction and the closing date, and placed in the designated box located on the first floor, reception hall, at the Company's Head Office building in Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig>, no later than 1:00 PM (13:00 PM) on Thursday, 4/17/2025.
- Please note that a preliminary remote meeting for bidders will be held (online via Microsoft Teams application) at 10:00 AM on Monday, 2/17/2025, to answer bidders' inquiries. The meeting link - and other details for joining the meeting - will be sent to all bidders through the e-Tendering portal (K-Tendering portal), which bidders should monitor periodically for updates regarding the auction.
- This auction is divisible, and alternative bids are not permitted.
- To obtain a username and password to access the e-Tendering portal, please contact the following phone numbers: 23887794 / 23887792.
- Bidders are required to submit the following documents:

# Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig>
## Announcement

Regarding the list of companies invited to participate in Limited Tender No. (P&MAB-01/2024)
The Higher Purchasing Committee for Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> Tenders, upon request from Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig> (KOTC) – one of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation's <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> companies – announces the list of companies invited to participate in Limited Tender No. P&MAB-01/2024, which is for providing specialized marine services with skilled labor for the Marine Agency Branch of Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig>.
In this regard, we draw attention to the fact that, based on Article (16) of Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning Public Tenders, the aforementioned tender will be offered to the following list of (22) companies at least (30) days from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette (Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) and on the website of Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig>. Any interested party whose name is not included in the list of companies invited to the tender has the right to appeal their exclusion or submit a request to participate in the tender, supported by relevant documents and addressed to Mr. / Chairman of the Higher Purchasing Committee for Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> Tenders and its subsidiaries, within (30) days from the date of this announcement.
An appellant whose name is not included in the above list, if submitting an appeal / participation request to the Board of Directors of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig>, must pay a fee of (K.D. 250) for appeal / participation requests, in consideration of reviewing the possibility of adding them to that list.
The appeal / participation request fee shall be paid by bank deposit slip into the Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig> account mentioned below, provided that the appeal fee shall be refunded to the contractor / supplier if their appeal is accepted formally and substantively.
National Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت الوطني</orig> - Main Branch - Kuwait
Account No.: 1000307805
IBAN: KW49NBOK000000000001000307805
SWIFT: NBOKKKW

## Announcement

S.C.C for Updating the Operating System at the Liquefied Gas Filling Branch (Shuaiba <orig>الشعيبية</orig>)
Reference No.: LPG-03/2024

The Higher Purchasing Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its Subsidiaries announces, based on the request of Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig>, the direct award of the contract for updating the operating system at the Liquefied Gas Filling Branch (Shuaiba <orig>الشعيبية</orig>) to Honeywell Kuwait K.S.C.C. for a total price of K.D. 244,772/- (Two Hundred Forty-Four Thousand Seven Hundred Seventy-Two Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> only) under a contract for a period of 12 months from the date of the commencement order.

2024/02/16 at the Liquefied Gas Filling Plant in Umm Al-Aish <orig>أم العيش</orig> area, affiliated with Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig>, with the necessity of sending the names of authorized representatives to attend the site visit via an official letter signed by the authorized signatory for the company in the tender, provided that copies of the civil IDs of the authorized representatives are attached for attendance, in order to obtain site entry permits two days prior to the visit date.
Note:
*   This tender is indivisible.
*   Bidders who have inquiries or reservations regarding the technical terms and specifications should note that the deadline for submitting their inquiries is Tuesday, 18/02/2025, at the latest.
*   Based on the text of Article (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016: -
*   A single person or a group of persons collectively may not register under more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, their engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may, during classification, register himself and each of his independent companies. The bid of a bidder who violates this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law.
*   No bidder will be allowed to attend the preliminary meeting unless proof of purchase of the tender documents is provided.
*   The bidder must submit the initial security deposit in favor of Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig>.
As for any inquiries regarding the data of the invited companies, bidders wishing to participate in the tender, if they have any inquiries regarding the KPC & Subsidiaries K-Tendering Portal (ktendering.com.kw) electronic system, should contact CPQ Helpdesk using the details provided below:
Phone: +965 23872333
Email: cpqhelpdesk@kockw.com

### Exclusion Announcement
Practice for the Supply of Marine Lubricants
Reference No.: FEG-06/2024

The Higher Purchasing Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its Subsidiaries announces the exclusion of the bid submitted by SHELL MARINE PRODUCTS SINGAPORE for FEG-06/2024 concerning the supply of marine lubricants, due to technical and commercial deviations and the company's inability to meet the technical and commercial requirements.

<header>

144
Sunday, 3 Sha'ban 1446 AH - 2/2/2025 AD
</header>

Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>, one of the Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> companies, announces the award of the public tender to the bid submitted by AL-ESSA TECHNICAL SERVICES FOR WHOLESALE AND RETAIL TRADING CO. W.L.L. at a maximum cost of K.D. 412,200 (Four Hundred Twelve Thousand Two Hundred Kuwaiti Dinars only), and whose offer complies with the conditions stipulated in the tender documents.

---

# Announcement of Postponement

Regarding the postponement of the preliminary meeting date
Concerning Tender No.: RFP-2114392
**RECRUITMENT OF PERSONNEL FROM OVERSEAS**

Further to the announcement published in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>), Issue No. (1720), Page No. (296) dated 5/1/2025, regarding the aforementioned tender.
The Higher Purchasing Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries wishes, upon the request of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>, to draw the attention of the esteemed bidders that the date of the preliminary meeting for the aforementioned tender has been postponed to 3/2/2025 instead of 28/1/2025.
Hence, this announcement is made.
For more details, please visit the official website of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> through the commercial electronic page (K-Tendering Portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:
https://www.ktendering.com.kw

---

# Announcement Regarding the List of Companies Invited to Participate in Limited Tender No.: RFP-2125792

The Internal Purchasing Committee at Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> announces the list of companies invited to participate in the limited tender
RFP-2125792:
**REPLACEMENT OF OBSOLETE FIRE**

# WATER PUMP CONTROL SYSTEM AT EXPORT FACILITIES (NTF & STF)

In this regard, we draw attention to the fact that, based on the text of Article (16) of Tenders Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning Public Tenders, the aforementioned tender will be issued to the following list of companies, at least (48) days from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) and on the company's website, and any interested party whose name is not included in the list of invited companies for the tender has the right to appeal their exclusion or submit a request to participate in the tender, supported by relevant documents, within (30) days from the date of this announcement.

Instructions to Applicants for Tenders based on Common Categories of Work
- The documents shall be submitted strictly in line with the published questionnaire along with the Expression of Interest letter in USB/CD only (hardcopy documents submission is not acceptable).
- Supporting documents shall be clearly segregated/organized as single file in respective sections – Commercial, Technical, HSE and Financial as applicable. Kuwait Oil Company will not take any responsibility in segregation of the Supporting Documents/Attachments.
- Password encrypted files, external internet links and Jpeg are not acceptable.
The application submission shall be final, complete and in line with the PQ questionnaire. Incomplete/Late submission shall not be accepted and will lead to disqualification of the same.

Announcement
Regarding the Award of Practice No.: RFP-2129185
LANDFILL INSPECTIONS,
MAINTENANCE AND MONITORING
(SK LANDFILLS)
Based on the approval of the Higher Purchasing Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries, in its meeting No. (8 / 2025) held on 21 / 01 / 2025.

SPECIALITIES CONSTRUCTION GENERAL
TRADING AND CONTRACTING
COMPANY W.L.L. at a maximum cost of (-/ USD 12,903,000) (Twelve Million Nine Hundred Three Thousand US Dollars only), which complies with the conditions stipulated in the practice documents.

https://www.ktendering.com.kw →
Opportunities → Current Opportunities →
Search for the RFP Title using the Filter.
Instructions clarifying how to participate and submit the required documents are as follows:
Existing business partners
Existing business partners who wish to participate in the subject Tender, shall kindly ensure that the account status is “ACTIVE” in the K-tendering portal.
New business partners
New business partners who wish to participate in the subject Tender, but not registered in K-Tendering Portal shall first complete their registration process and ensure that their account status is “ACTIVE” before applying/submitting their Expression of Interest. For registration in K-Tendering Portal navigate to https://ktendering.com.kw → Click on Supplier Registration → Apply for Registration. For more information, please visit https://ktendering.com.kw or contact us vide email at ktendering@kockw.com or by calling: +965 238 72333.
Note: Expression of Interest from non-registered entities shall not be accepted.

Announcement
Regarding the Issuance of Tender No.: RFP-2140459
PROVISION OF ULTRAWIDE FIELD OCT AND ANGIOGRAPHY SYSTEM COMPLETE WITH ALL STANDARD ACCESSORIES

Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> announces the issuance of the above-mentioned tender in accordance with the terms and specifications contained in the tender documents. Tender documents can be viewed or obtained, or any additional information can be found by visiting the Unified Commercial Electronic Platform (K-Tendering Portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:
- This is a general tender, noting that it will include specific terms and criteria and meet the technical requirements stated in the tender documents.
- Based on the text of Article (29) of Law No. 49 of 2016 <orig>قانون رقم 49 لسنة 2016</orig> regarding Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>, it is not permissible for one person or a group of persons collectively to register under more than one name during classification or to submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions allow their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent with its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may register himself and each of his independent companies during classification. The bid of a bidder who violates this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law.
- Companies wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, etc., must adhere to submitting them to the relevant authority by the deadline.

Announcement
Regarding the List of Companies Invited to Participate in Limited Tender No.: RFP-2142697
The Higher Purchasing Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries, upon the request of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>, announces the list of companies invited to participate in Limited Tender:
No.: RFP-2142697
CONSTRUCTION OF NEW OFFICE
COMPLEX IN AHMADI
(BUILDING 2 – 400 OFFICES)
In this regard, we draw attention to the fact that, based on the text of Article (16) of Tenders Law No. (49) of 2016 concerning Public Tenders <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة</orig>, the aforementioned tender will be offered to the following list of (13) companies at least (30) days from the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) and on the company's website. Any interested party whose name is not included in the list of invited companies for the tender has the right to submit a request for exclusion or to submit a request to participate in the tender, supported by relevant documents and addressed to Mr. / Chairman of the Higher Purchasing Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries, within (30) days from the date of this announcement:

- This tender is general for all suppliers, non-divisible, provided that the required materials have been approved in the unified category of the Central Qualification Committee <orig>لجنة التأهيل المركزية</orig> as stated in the tender documents.
- Based on the text of Article (29) of Law No. 49 of 2016 <orig>قانون رقم 49 لسنة 2016</orig> regarding Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>: "No single person or group of persons collectively may register under more than one name when classified, or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission. As for a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent with its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, they may register themselves and each of their independent companies when classified. Any bid from a tenderer violating this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law."
- The tenderer must deposit the tender document purchase fee into the Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> account mentioned below, with the necessity of adding the tender number and company name to the bank-issued purchase receipt and submitting the receipt with the bid. - Pursuant to the text of Article (29) of Law No. 49 of 2016 regarding Public Tenders <orig>قانون رقم 49 لسنة 2016 بشأن المناقصات العامة</orig>, "No single person or group of persons combined may register under classification with more than one name or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each with its own legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may register himself and each of his independent companies under classification. The bid of a tenderer who violates this Article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law."
- The tenderer must deposit the tender document purchase fee into the Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> account mentioned below, with the necessity of adding the tender number and purchase name to the purchase receipt issued by the bank and submitting the receipt with the bid. Bids not accompanied by a payment receipt will be excluded. In case of electronic bid submission, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached electronically with the bid:
  - **BANK NAME:** NATIONAL BANK OF KUWAIT, AHMADI BRANCH

  - **OR**

- A certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> and valid for one year, must be attached with the bid.
- Companies wishing to participate in this tender, and which meet the required specifications and criteria in the tender documents, must be registered on the Unified Electronic Commercial Platform (K-Tendering Portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:
